<script>
// STATE & STORAGE
let S={pan:null,members:{},theme:'system'};
let donutChart=null;
let selFund=null,selStock=null;
let editMFi=null,editSTi=null,editBNDi=null,editBNKi=null;
let mfDebT=null,stkDebT=null;
let panVis=false,panPVis=false;
let pendingCAS=null,pendingDemat=null,pendingBroker=null,pendingBonds=null,pendingBank=null;

function persist(){try{localStorage.setItem(STORE,JSON.stringify(S));}catch(e){toast('Storage full — export a backup','err');}}
function hydrate(){try{const d=localStorage.getItem(STORE);if(d){const p=JSON.parse(d);if(p&&typeof p==='object')S=Object.assign({pan:null,members:{},theme:'system'},p);}}catch(e){S={pan:null,members:{},theme:'system'};}}
hydrate();

const g=id=>document.getElementById(id);
const sf=(v,fb=0)=>{const n=parseFloat(v);return(isFinite(n)&&!isNaN(n))?n:fb;};
const wait=ms=>new Promise(r=>setTimeout(r,ms));

function cm(){
  if(!S.pan||!S.members[S.pan])return{holdings:[],stocks:[],insurance:[],bonds:[],bankAccounts:[]};
  const m=S.members[S.pan];
  if(!Array.isArray(m.holdings))m.holdings=[];
  if(!Array.isArray(m.stocks))m.stocks=[];
  if(!Array.isArray(m.insurance))m.insurance=[];
  if(!Array.isArray(m.bonds))m.bonds=[];
  if(!Array.isArray(m.bankAccounts))m.bankAccounts=[];
  return m;
}

function fm(n,d=2){if(n==null||!isFinite(n))return'—';return new Intl.NumberFormat('en-IN',{minimumFractionDigits:d,maximumFractionDigits:d}).format(n);}
function fL(n){
  if(!isFinite(n)||n==null)return RU+'0';
  const a=Math.abs(n),s=n<0?'-':'';
  if(a>=1e7)return s+RU+fm(a/1e7,2)+' Cr';
  if(a>=1e5)return s+RU+fm(a/1e5,2)+' L';
  return s+RU+fm(a,0);
}
function nowStr(){return new Date().toLocaleString('en-IN',{day:'2-digit',month:'short',year:'numeric',hour:'2-digit',minute:'2-digit'});}

// THEME
function setTheme(t){
  S.theme=t;
  document.documentElement.setAttribute('data-theme',t);
  ['light','dark'].forEach(k=>{const btn=g('tt-'+k);if(btn)btn.classList.toggle('active',k===t);});
  if(donutChart){donutChart.destroy();donutChart=null;renderPortfolio();}
  persist();
}
(function(){
  const t=(S.theme&&S.theme!=='system')?S.theme:'light';
  document.documentElement.setAttribute('data-theme',t);
  ['light','dark'].forEach(k=>{const btn=g('tt-'+k);if(btn)btn.classList.toggle('active',k===t);});
})();

// LOGIN / LOGOUT
function doLogin(){
  const pan=(g('l-pan').value||'').trim().toUpperCase();
  const name=(g('l-name').value||'').trim()||'User';
  if(!/^[A-Z]{5}[0-9]{4}[A-Z]$/.test(pan)){toast('Enter valid 10-char PAN','err');return;}
  if(!S.members[pan])S.members[pan]={name,pan,rel:'Self',holdings:[],stocks:[],insurance:[],bonds:[],bankAccounts:[],lastUpdated:null};
  else S.members[pan].name=name;
  S.pan=pan;persist();
  g('login-screen').style.display='none';g('app-screen').style.display='block';
  g('tb-name').textContent=name.split(' ')[0];g('tb-pan').textContent=maskPAN(pan);panVis=false;
  setTheme((S.theme&&S.theme!=='system')?S.theme:'light');
  selP('mfc');renderAll();
  const m=cm();
  if((m.holdings||[]).length||(m.stocks||[]).length)refreshAll(true);
}

function doLogout(){
  S.pan=null;persist();
  if(donutChart){donutChart.destroy();donutChart=null;}
  selFund=null;selStock=null;editMFi=null;editSTi=null;editBNDi=null;editBNKi=null;
  panVis=false;pendingCAS=null;pendingDemat=null;pendingBroker=null;pendingBonds=null;pendingBank=null;
  document.querySelectorAll('.ov.open').forEach(e=>e.classList.remove('open'));
  g('app-screen').style.display='none';g('login-screen').style.display='flex';
  g('l-pan').value='';g('l-name').value='';
  toast('Logged out','ok');
}
const maskPAN=p=>!p?'••••••••••':p.slice(0,2)+'••••••'+p.slice(-2);
function togglePAN(){panVis=!panVis;g('tb-pan').textContent=panVis?S.pan:maskPAN(S.pan);}
function togglePANPro(){panPVis=!panPVis;g('pro-pan').textContent=panPVis?S.pan:maskPAN(S.pan);g('pro-pan-btn').textContent=panPVis?'Hide PAN':'Show PAN';}
</script>


<script>
// RENDER ALL
function renderAll(){
  try{renderPortfolio();}catch(e){console.error('renderPortfolio:',e);}
  try{renderFamily();}catch(e){console.error('renderFamily:',e);}
  try{renderInsurance();}catch(e){console.error('renderInsurance:',e);}
  try{renderBanks();}catch(e){console.error('renderBanks:',e);}
  try{renderProfile();}catch(e){console.error('renderProfile:',e);}
}

function renderPortfolio(){
  const m=cm();
  const mf=m.holdings||[],sk=m.stocks||[],bnd=m.bonds||[];
  let mfI=0,mfC=0,mfP=0;
  for(const f of mf){const u=sf(f.units),a=sf(f.avgNav),c=sf(f.currentNav)>0?sf(f.currentNav):a,p=sf(f.prevNav)>0?sf(f.prevNav):c;mfI+=u*a;mfC+=u*c;mfP+=u*p;}
  let skI=0,skC=0,skP=0;
  for(const s of sk){const q=sf(s.qty),a=sf(s.avgPrice),c=sf(s.currentPrice)>0?sf(s.currentPrice):a,p=sf(s.prevPrice)>0?sf(s.prevPrice):c;skI+=q*a;skC+=q*c;skP+=q*p;}
  let bndI=0,bndC=0;
  for(const b of bnd){const inv=sf(b.qty)*sf(b.purchasePrice);bndI+=inv;bndC+=inv;}// bonds at cost (no live price)
  const tI=mfI+skI+bndI,tC=mfC+skC+bndC,tP=mfP+skP+bndC;
  const gain=tC-tI,ret=tI>0?gain/tI*100:0,d1=tC-tP,d1p=tP>0?d1/tP*100:0;

  g('s-total').innerHTML=`<span class="ru ru-lg">ரூ</span>${fL(tC).replace(RU,'')}`;
  g('s-inv').innerHTML=`<span class="ru">ரூ</span>${fL(tI).replace(RU,'')}`;
  g('s-cnt').textContent=`${mf.length} fund${mf.length!==1?'s':''} · ${sk.length} stock${sk.length!==1?'s':''} · ${bnd.length} bond${bnd.length!==1?'s':''}`;
  g('s-ret').textContent=(ret>=0?'+':'')+fm(ret,2)+'%';
  g('s-ret').style.color=ret>=0?'var(--grn)':'var(--rose)';
  g('s-ret-s').innerHTML=`<span style="color:var(--tx3)">gain: </span><span style="color:${gain>=0?'var(--grn)':'var(--rose)'}">${gain>=0?'+':'-'}${fL(Math.abs(gain))}</span>`;
  g('s-1d').innerHTML=`<span class="ru">ரூ</span>${fL(Math.abs(d1)).replace(RU,'')}`;
  g('s-1d').style.color=d1>=0?'var(--grn)':'var(--rose)';
  g('s-1d-s').innerHTML=`<span class="${d1>=0?'up':'dn2'}">${(d1p>=0?'+':'')+fm(d1p,2)}%</span>`;
  const chip=g('s-chip');chip.className='pill '+(gain>=0?'pill-up':'pill-dn');
  chip.textContent=(gain>=0?'▲ ':'▼ ')+fm(Math.abs(ret),2)+'%';
  g('s-gain-txt').style.color=gain>=0?'var(--grn)':'var(--rose)';
  g('s-gain-txt').textContent=(gain>=0?' +':' -')+fL(Math.abs(gain));
  renderDonut(mf,sk,bnd);renderMFTable(mf);renderStkTable(sk);renderBndTable(bnd);
  if(m.lastUpdated)g('last-upd').textContent='Updated: '+m.lastUpdated;
}

function renderDonut(mf,sk,bnd){
  const tot=mf.length+sk.length+(bnd||[]).length;
  g('dc-n').textContent=tot;
  const barsEl=g('alloc-bars'),dcV=g('dc-v');
  if(!tot){if(donutChart){donutChart.destroy();donutChart=null;}if(barsEl)barsEl.innerHTML='';if(dcV)dcV.textContent='';return;}
  const cats={};
  for(const f of mf){const cat=getCat(f.category,f.name),fNav=sf(f.currentNav)>0?sf(f.currentNav):sf(f.avgNav),v=sf(f.units)*fNav;if(v>0)cats[cat]=(cats[cat]||0)+v;}
  for(const s of sk){const sPrice=sf(s.currentPrice)>0?sf(s.currentPrice):sf(s.avgPrice),v=sf(s.qty)*sPrice;if(v>0)cats['Stocks']=(cats['Stocks']||0)+v;}
  for(const b of (bnd||[])){const v=sf(b.qty)*sf(b.purchasePrice);if(v>0)cats['Bonds']=(cats['Bonds']||0)+v;}
  if(!Object.keys(cats).length){if(donutChart){donutChart.destroy();donutChart=null;}if(barsEl)barsEl.innerHTML='';if(dcV)dcV.textContent='';return;}
  const entries=Object.entries(cats).sort((a,b)=>b[1]-a[1]);
  const lb=entries.map(e=>e[0]),dv=entries.map(e=>e[1]),tt=dv.reduce((a,b)=>a+b,0)||1;
  const RICH_PAL=['#4f52d6','#0f9b6e','#c96c0b','#dc2c4a','#0679b8','#6c28d9','#0a8a82','#16a34a','#db2777','#0891b2','#7c3aed','#b45309','#0e7490','#be185d','#047857','#7e22ce'];
  const col=lb.map((_,i)=>RICH_PAL[i%RICH_PAL.length]);
  if(dcV)dcV.textContent=fL(tt);
  if(donutChart)donutChart.destroy();
  donutChart=new Chart(g('donut').getContext('2d'),{type:'doughnut',data:{labels:lb,datasets:[{data:dv,backgroundColor:col,borderWidth:2,borderColor:'var(--bg2)',hoverOffset:8,hoverBorderWidth:0}]},options:{cutout:'70%',plugins:{legend:{display:false},tooltip:{callbacks:{label:i=>` ${fm(i.raw/tt*100,1)}%  ·  ${fL(i.raw)}`},backgroundColor:'var(--bg2)',titleColor:'var(--tx)',bodyColor:'var(--tx2)',borderColor:'var(--bdr2)',borderWidth:1,padding:10,cornerRadius:8}},animation:{duration:500,easing:'easeInOutQuart'}}});
  if(!barsEl)return;
  const maxVal=dv[0]||1;
  barsEl.innerHTML=entries.map(([lbl,val],i)=>{const pct=(val/tt*100).toFixed(1),barW=(val/maxVal*100).toFixed(1);return`<div class="ab-row"><div class="ab-top"><div class="ab-lbl"><div class="ab-dot" style="background:${col[i]}"></div><span>${escH(lbl)}</span></div><div style="display:flex;gap:8px;align-items:center"><span class="ab-val">${fL(val)}</span><span class="ab-pct">${pct}%</span></div></div><div class="ab-track"><div class="ab-fill" style="background:${col[i]};width:0" data-w="${barW}%"></div></div></div>`;}).join('')+`<div class="alloc-total-row"><span>${tot} position${tot!==1?'s':''}</span><span>${fL(tt)} total</span></div>`;
  requestAnimationFrame(()=>requestAnimationFrame(()=>barsEl.querySelectorAll('.ab-fill').forEach(el=>el.style.width=el.dataset.w)));
}

function renderMFTable(mf){
  const e=!mf.length;g('mf-empty').style.display=e?'block':'none';g('mf-tbl').style.display=e?'none':'table';g('mf-sel-btn').style.display=e?'none':'inline-flex';if(e)return;
  // compute section totals for header
  let totInv=0,totCur=0,totGn=0;
  for(const f of mf){const u=sf(f.units),a=sf(f.avgNav),c=sf(f.currentNav)>0?sf(f.currentNav):a;totInv+=u*a;totCur+=u*c;}
  totGn=totCur-totInv;
  const totRt=totInv>0?totGn/totInv*100:0;
  // Update panel stats bar if exists
  const sb=g('mf-stats-bar');
  if(sb){sb.style.display='flex';sb.innerHTML=`<div class="sec-stat"><div class="sec-stat-l">Invested</div><div class="sec-stat-v" style="color:var(--tx)">${fL(totInv)}</div></div><div class="sec-stat"><div class="sec-stat-l">Market Value</div><div class="sec-stat-v" style="color:var(--ind)">${fL(totCur)}</div></div><div class="sec-stat"><div class="sec-stat-l">Gain/Loss</div><div class="sec-stat-v" style="color:${totGn>=0?'var(--grn)':'var(--rose)'}">${totGn>=0?'+':''}${fL(totGn)}</div></div><div class="sec-stat"><div class="sec-stat-l">Return</div><div class="sec-stat-v" style="color:${totRt>=0?'var(--grn)':'var(--rose)'}">${totRt>=0?'+':''}${fm(totRt,2)}%</div></div><div class="sec-stat"><div class="sec-stat-l">Funds</div><div class="sec-stat-v">${mf.length}</div></div>`;}
  g('mf-body').innerHTML=mf.map((f,i)=>{
    const u=sf(f.units),a=sf(f.avgNav),c=sf(f.currentNav)>0?sf(f.currentNav):a,p=sf(f.prevNav)>0?sf(f.prevNav):c,vi=u*a,vc=u*c,gn=vc-vi,rt=vi>0?gn/vi*100:0,dp=p>0&&p!==c?(c-p)/p*100:0;
    return`<tr>
      <td><input type="checkbox" class="mf-chk" data-i="${i}" onchange="updMFSel()" style="cursor:pointer"></td>
      <td><div class="fn" title="${escH(f.name)}">${escH(f.name.length>44?f.name.slice(0,44)+'…':f.name)}</div>
          <div class="fn-sub"><span class="tag ti">${getCat(f.category,f.name)}</span>${f.folio?`<span class="ts">Folio: ${escH(f.folio)}</span>`:''}</div></td>
      <td><div class="ts" style="font-family:'JetBrains Mono',monospace;font-size:10.5px;color:var(--tx2)">${f.amfiCode||'—'}</div></td>
      <td><div class="val-main gld">${fm(c,4)}</div>${f.navDate?`<div class="val-sub">${f.navDate}</div>`:''}</td>
      <td><div class="val-main">${fm(u,4)}</div></td>
      <td><div class="val-main">${fL(vi)}</div></td>
      <td><div class="val-main" style="color:var(--ind)">${fL(vc)}</div></td>
      <td><div class="val-main ${gn>=0?'up':'dn2'}">${gn>=0?'+':''}${fL(gn)}</div></td>
      <td><span class="mo ${rt>=0?'up':'dn2'}" style="font-size:13px">${rt>=0?'+':''}${fm(rt,2)}%</span></td>
      <td><span class="mo ${dp>=0?'up':'dn2'}" style="font-size:13px">${dp>=0?'+':''}${fm(dp,2)}%</span></td>
      <td style="white-space:nowrap"><button class="btn btn-g btn-sm" onclick="editMF(${i})">✎</button> <button class="btn btn-d btn-sm" onclick="delMF(${i})">✕</button></td>
    </tr>`;
  }).join('');
}

function renderStkTable(sk){
  const e=!sk.length;g('stk-empty').style.display=e?'block':'none';g('stk-tbl').style.display=e?'none':'table';g('stk-sel-btn').style.display=e?'none':'inline-flex';if(e)return;
  // totals
  let totInv=0,totCur=0;
  for(const s of sk){const q=sf(s.qty),a=sf(s.avgPrice),c=sf(s.currentPrice)>0?sf(s.currentPrice):a;totInv+=q*a;totCur+=q*c;}
  const totGn=totCur-totInv,totRt=totInv>0?totGn/totInv*100:0;
  const sb=g('stk-stats-bar');
  if(sb){sb.style.display='flex';sb.innerHTML=`<div class="sec-stat"><div class="sec-stat-l">Invested</div><div class="sec-stat-v" style="color:var(--tx)">${fL(totInv)}</div></div><div class="sec-stat"><div class="sec-stat-l">Market Value</div><div class="sec-stat-v" style="color:var(--ind)">${fL(totCur)}</div></div><div class="sec-stat"><div class="sec-stat-l">Gain/Loss</div><div class="sec-stat-v" style="color:${totGn>=0?'var(--grn)':'var(--rose)'}">${totGn>=0?'+':''}${fL(totGn)}</div></div><div class="sec-stat"><div class="sec-stat-l">Return</div><div class="sec-stat-v" style="color:${totRt>=0?'var(--grn)':'var(--rose)'}">${totRt>=0?'+':''}${fm(totRt,2)}%</div></div><div class="sec-stat"><div class="sec-stat-l">Stocks</div><div class="sec-stat-v">${sk.length}</div></div>`;}
  g('stk-body').innerHTML=sk.map((s,i)=>{
    const q=sf(s.qty),a=sf(s.avgPrice),c=sf(s.currentPrice)>0?sf(s.currentPrice):a,p=sf(s.prevPrice)>0?sf(s.prevPrice):c,vi=q*a,vc=q*c,gn=vc-vi,rt=vi>0?gn/vi*100:0,dp=p>0&&p!==c?(c-p)/p*100:0;
    const priceCell=s.liveOk
      ?`<div class="val-main gld price-live">${fm(c,2)}</div>${s.lastFetch?`<div class="val-sub">Live · ${s.lastFetch} · ${escH(s.priceSource||'')}</div>`:''}`
      :`<div class="val-main" style="color:var(--amb)">${fm(a||c,2)}</div><div class="val-sub">avg cost · tap ↻</div>`;
    const brokerTag=s.broker?`<span class="tag ti" style="font-size:9px">${escH(s.broker)}</span>`:'';
    return`<tr>
      <td><input type="checkbox" class="stk-chk" data-i="${i}" onchange="updStkSel()" style="cursor:pointer"></td>
      <td><div class="fn">${escH(s.name||s.ticker)}</div>
          <div class="fn-sub">${brokerTag}${s.buyDate?`<span class="ts">Bought: ${s.buyDate}</span>`:''}</div></td>
      <td><div style="font-family:'JetBrains Mono',monospace;font-size:12px;color:var(--ind);font-weight:800">${escH(s.ticker)}</div>
          <div class="val-sub">${s.exchange||'NSE'}</div></td>
      <td><div class="isin-code" style="font-size:11px">${s.isin||'—'}</div></td>
      <td><div class="val-main">${q}</div></td>
      <td><div class="val-main">${fm(a,2)}</div></td>
      <td>${priceCell}</td>
      <td><div class="val-main">${fL(vi)}</div></td>
      <td><div class="val-main" style="color:var(--ind)">${fL(vc)}</div></td>
      <td><div class="val-main ${gn>=0?'up':'dn2'}">${gn>=0?'+':''}${fL(gn)}</div></td>
      <td><span class="mo ${rt>=0?'up':'dn2'}" style="font-size:13px">${rt>=0?'+':''}${fm(rt,2)}%</span></td>
      <td><span class="mo ${dp>=0?'up':'dn2'}" style="font-size:13px">${dp>=0?'+':''}${fm(dp,2)}%</span></td>
      <td style="white-space:nowrap"><button class="btn btn-g btn-sm" onclick="editStk(${i})">✎</button> <button class="btn btn-d btn-sm" onclick="delStk(${i})">✕</button></td>
    </tr>`;
  }).join('');
}

function renderBndTable(bnd){
  const e=!bnd.length;g('bnd-empty').style.display=e?'block':'none';g('bnd-tbl').style.display=e?'none':'table';g('bnd-sel-btn').style.display=e?'none':'inline-flex';if(e)return;
  // totals
  let totInv=0;for(const b of bnd)totInv+=sf(b.qty)*sf(b.purchasePrice);
  const sb=g('bnd-stats-bar');
  if(sb){sb.style.display='flex';sb.innerHTML=`<div class="sec-stat"><div class="sec-stat-l">Total Invested</div><div class="sec-stat-v" style="color:var(--ind)">${fL(totInv)}</div></div><div class="sec-stat"><div class="sec-stat-l">Bonds</div><div class="sec-stat-v">${bnd.length}</div></div>`;}
  const today=new Date();
  g('bnd-body').innerHTML=bnd.map((b,i)=>{
    const invested=sf(b.qty)*sf(b.purchasePrice);
    const matDiff=b.maturityDate?Math.ceil((new Date(b.maturityDate)-today)/864e5):null;
    const matCls=matDiff===null?'':matDiff<0?'dn2':matDiff<90?'up':'gld';
    const tc=BOND_COL[b.type]||'var(--tx3)';
    return`<tr>
      <td><input type="checkbox" class="bnd-chk" data-i="${i}" onchange="updBndSel()" style="cursor:pointer"></td>
      <td><div class="fn" title="${escH(b.name)}">${escH(b.name.length>40?b.name.slice(0,40)+'…':b.name)}</div>
          <div class="fn-sub">${b.platform?`<span class="ts">${escH(b.platform)}</span>`:''}</div></td>
      <td><span class="tag tt2" style="background:${tc}22;color:${tc};font-size:10px">${BOND_LBL[b.type]||'Bond'}</span></td>
      <td><div class="isin-code" style="font-size:11px">${b.isin||'—'}</div></td>
      <td><div class="val-main">${sf(b.qty)}</div></td>
      <td><div class="val-main">${fL(sf(b.faceValue))}</div></td>
      <td><div class="val-main" style="color:var(--ind)">${fL(invested)}</div></td>
      <td><div class="val-main gld">${b.couponRate?fm(b.couponRate,2)+'%':'—'}</div></td>
      <td><div style="font-size:12px;font-weight:700;color:${b.rating==='AAA'||b.rating==='Sovereign'?'var(--grn)':b.rating&&b.rating.includes('-')?'var(--amb)':'var(--tx)'}">${b.rating||'—'}</div></td>
      <td><div class="ts" style="font-size:11px">${b.investDate||'—'}</div></td>
      <td><div class="val-main ${matCls}" style="font-size:12px">${b.maturityDate||'—'}</div>${matDiff!==null&&matDiff>=0?`<div class="val-sub">${matDiff<365?matDiff+'d left':Math.floor(matDiff/365)+'y left'}</div>`:''}</td>
      <td style="white-space:nowrap"><button class="btn btn-g btn-sm" onclick="editBond(${i})">✎</button> <button class="btn btn-d btn-sm" onclick="delBond(${i})">✕</button></td>
    </tr>`;
  }).join('');
}

function escH(s){return String(s||'').replace(/&/g,'&amp;').replace(/</g,'&lt;').replace(/>/g,'&gt;').replace(/"/g,'&quot;');}
</script>


<script>
// SELECT / DELETE HELPERS
function toggleAllMF(){const all=[...document.querySelectorAll('.mf-chk')].every(c=>c.checked);document.querySelectorAll('.mf-chk').forEach(c=>c.checked=!all);const ca=g('mf-chk-all');if(ca)ca.checked=!all;updMFSel();}
function mfChkAll(v){document.querySelectorAll('.mf-chk').forEach(c=>c.checked=v);updMFSel();}
function updMFSel(){const n=[...document.querySelectorAll('.mf-chk:checked')].length;const db=g('mf-del-btn');if(db){db.style.display=n?'inline-flex':'none';if(n)db.textContent=`Delete ${n}`;}const ca=g('mf-chk-all');if(ca)ca.checked=n>0&&n===document.querySelectorAll('.mf-chk').length;}
function delSelectedMF(){const idx=[...document.querySelectorAll('.mf-chk:checked')].map(c=>+c.dataset.i).sort((a,b)=>b-a);if(!idx.length||!confirm(`Remove ${idx.length} fund${idx.length>1?'s':''}?`))return;idx.forEach(i=>cm().holdings.splice(i,1));persist();renderAll();toast(`${idx.length} fund${idx.length>1?'s':''} removed`,'ok');}
function delMF(i){if(!confirm('Remove this fund?'))return;cm().holdings.splice(i,1);persist();renderAll();toast('Fund removed','ok');}

function toggleAllStk(){const all=[...document.querySelectorAll('.stk-chk')].every(c=>c.checked);document.querySelectorAll('.stk-chk').forEach(c=>c.checked=!all);const ca=g('stk-chk-all');if(ca)ca.checked=!all;updStkSel();}
function stkChkAll(v){document.querySelectorAll('.stk-chk').forEach(c=>c.checked=v);updStkSel();}
function updStkSel(){const n=[...document.querySelectorAll('.stk-chk:checked')].length;const db=g('stk-del-btn');if(db){db.style.display=n?'inline-flex':'none';if(n)db.textContent=`Delete ${n}`;}const ca=g('stk-chk-all');if(ca)ca.checked=n>0&&n===document.querySelectorAll('.stk-chk').length;}
function delSelectedStk(){const idx=[...document.querySelectorAll('.stk-chk:checked')].map(c=>+c.dataset.i).sort((a,b)=>b-a);if(!idx.length||!confirm(`Remove ${idx.length} stock${idx.length>1?'s':''}?`))return;idx.forEach(i=>cm().stocks.splice(i,1));persist();renderAll();toast(`${idx.length} stock${idx.length>1?'s':''} removed`,'ok');}
function delStk(i){if(!confirm('Remove this stock?'))return;cm().stocks.splice(i,1);persist();renderAll();toast('Stock removed','ok');}

function toggleAllBnd(){const all=[...document.querySelectorAll('.bnd-chk')].every(c=>c.checked);document.querySelectorAll('.bnd-chk').forEach(c=>c.checked=!all);const ca=g('bnd-chk-all');if(ca)ca.checked=!all;updBndSel();}
function bndChkAll(v){document.querySelectorAll('.bnd-chk').forEach(c=>c.checked=v);updBndSel();}
function updBndSel(){const n=[...document.querySelectorAll('.bnd-chk:checked')].length;const db=g('bnd-del-btn');if(db){db.style.display=n?'inline-flex':'none';if(n)db.textContent=`Delete ${n}`;}const ca=g('bnd-chk-all');if(ca)ca.checked=n>0&&n===document.querySelectorAll('.bnd-chk').length;}
function delSelectedBnd(){const idx=[...document.querySelectorAll('.bnd-chk:checked')].map(c=>+c.dataset.i).sort((a,b)=>b-a);if(!idx.length||!confirm(`Remove ${idx.length} bond${idx.length>1?'s':''}?`))return;idx.forEach(i=>cm().bonds.splice(i,1));persist();renderAll();toast(`${idx.length} bond${idx.length>1?'s':''} removed`,'ok');}
function delBond(i){if(!confirm('Remove this bond?'))return;cm().bonds.splice(i,1);persist();renderAll();toast('Bond removed','ok');}

// REFRESH
async function refreshAll(silent=false){
  const m=cm();
  if(!m.holdings.length&&!m.stocks.length){if(!silent)toast('No holdings to refresh','info');return;}
  const btn=g('ref-btn'),ico=g('ref-ico');
  if(ico)ico.classList.add('spin');if(btn)btn.disabled=true;
  if(!silent)toast('Refreshing NAVs & live prices…','info');
  let mfOk=0,mfFail=0;
  for(const h of m.holdings){
    if(!h.amfiCode){const c=await findAmfiCode(h.name);if(c)h.amfiCode=c;}
    if(h.amfiCode){const nd=await fetchNAV(h.amfiCode);if(nd){h.currentNav=nd.nav;h.prevNav=nd.prev;h.navDate=nd.date;if(nd.cat)h.category=nd.cat;mfOk++;}else mfFail++;}
    else mfFail++;
    await wait(200);
  }
  let skOk=0,skFail=0;
  for(const s of m.stocks){
    const r=await fetchStockPrice(s.ticker,s.isin,s.name);
    if(r&&r.price>0){s.currentPrice=r.price;s.prevPrice=r.prev;s.lastFetch=r.ts;s.liveOk=true;s.priceSource=r.source;skOk++;}
    else{s.liveOk=false;s.priceSource=null;skFail++;}
    renderStkTable(m.stocks);persist();await wait(400);
  }
  m.lastUpdated=nowStr();persist();renderAll();
  if(ico)ico.classList.remove('spin');if(btn)btn.disabled=false;
  const parts=[];
  if(mfOk)parts.push(`${mfOk} NAV${mfOk>1?'s':''} ✓`);
  if(skOk)parts.push(`${skOk} stock${skOk>1?'s':''} ✓`);
  if(mfFail)parts.push(`${mfFail} MF failed`);
  if(skFail)parts.push(`${skFail} stock unavailable`);
  toast(parts.join(' · ')||'Nothing updated',(mfOk+skOk)===0?'err':'ok');
}

async function refreshStocksOnly(){
  const m=cm();if(!m.stocks.length){toast('No stocks','info');return;}
  toast('Fetching live prices…','info');let ok=0,fail=0;
  for(const s of m.stocks){
    const r=await fetchStockPrice(s.ticker,s.isin,s.name);
    if(r&&r.price>0){s.currentPrice=r.price;s.prevPrice=r.prev;s.lastFetch=r.ts;s.liveOk=true;s.priceSource=r.source;ok++;}
    else{s.liveOk=false;s.priceSource=null;fail++;}
    renderStkTable(m.stocks);persist();await wait(400);
  }
  renderPortfolio();toast(`${ok} stock${ok!==1?'s':''} updated${fail?`, ${fail} unavailable`:''}`,ok>0?'ok':'err');
}
</script>


<script>
// AMFI NAV
async function fetchNAV(code){
  if(!code)return null;
  // 2 direct attempts
  for(let attempt=0;attempt<2;attempt++){
    try{
      const r=await fetch(`https://api.mfapi.in/mf/${code}`,{signal:AbortSignal.timeout(11000)});
      if(!r.ok)throw new Error('http');
      const d=await r.json();
      const e=Array.isArray(d.data)?d.data:[];if(!e.length)throw new Error('empty');
      const nav=parseFloat(e[0].nav);if(!isFinite(nav)||nav<=0)throw new Error('invalid');
      const prev=e.length>1?parseFloat(e[1].nav):nav;
      return{nav,prev:isFinite(prev)&&prev>0?prev:nav,date:e[0].date||'',cat:d.meta?.scheme_category||''};
    }catch{if(attempt===0)await wait(700);}
  }
  // CORS proxy fallback
  for(const mkP of PROXIES.slice(0,3)){
    try{
      const r=await fetch(mkP(`https://api.mfapi.in/mf/${code}`),{signal:AbortSignal.timeout(13000)});
      if(!r.ok)continue;
      const wrap=await r.json();
      const body=unwrapProxy(wrap);
      const obj=typeof body==='string'?JSON.parse(body):body;
      const e=Array.isArray(obj?.data)?obj.data:[];if(!e.length)continue;
      const nav=parseFloat(e[0].nav);if(!isFinite(nav)||nav<=0)continue;
      const prev=e.length>1?parseFloat(e[1].nav):nav;
      return{nav,prev:isFinite(prev)&&prev>0?prev:nav,date:e[0].date||'',cat:obj?.meta?.scheme_category||''};
    }catch{}
  }
  return null;
}
async function findAmfiCode(name){
  try{
    if(!name)return null;
    const q=name.trim().split(/\s+/).slice(0,6).join(' ');
    const r=await fetch(`https://api.mfapi.in/mf/search?q=${encodeURIComponent(q)}`,{signal:AbortSignal.timeout(8000)});
    const rs=await r.json();if(!Array.isArray(rs)||!rs.length)return null;
    for(const x of rs){const n=(x.schemeName||'').toUpperCase();if(n.includes('DIRECT')&&(n.includes('GROWTH')||n.includes(' GR ')))return String(x.schemeCode);}
    return String(rs[0].schemeCode);
  }catch{return null;}
}

// ── CORS PROXY CHAIN — ordered by reliability ──
const PROXIES=[
  u=>`https://api.allorigins.win/get?url=${encodeURIComponent(u)}`,
  u=>`https://api.codetabs.com/v1/proxy/?quest=${encodeURIComponent(u)}`,
  u=>`https://thingproxy.freeboard.io/fetch/${u}`,
];

function unwrapProxy(raw){
  if(!raw)return null;
  if(typeof raw==='object'&&raw.contents!==undefined){
    const c=raw.contents;try{return typeof c==='string'?JSON.parse(c):c;}catch{return c;}
  }
  return raw;
}
async function tryProxies(url,timeout=11000){
  for(const mkP of PROXIES){
    try{const r=await fetch(mkP(url),{signal:AbortSignal.timeout(timeout)});if(!r.ok)continue;return unwrapProxy(await r.json());}catch{}
  }
  return null;
}

// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// PRIMARY: MoneyControl Direct API — NO CORS PROXY NEEDED
// Works exactly like api.mfapi.in: direct browser fetch with CORS *
// Step 1: Search ISIN/ticker → get sc_id
// Step 2: Fetch live price using sc_id
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

async function mcSearch(query){
  // Returns {sc_id, name} or null
  if(!query||query.length<2)return null;
  try{
    const url=`https://www.moneycontrol.com/mccode/common/autosuggestion_solr.php?classic=true&query=${encodeURIComponent(query)}&type=1&format=json`;
    const r=await fetch(url,{signal:AbortSignal.timeout(8000)});
    if(!r.ok)return null;
    const data=await r.json();
    if(!Array.isArray(data)||!data.length)return null;
    const item=data[0];
    return{sc_id:item.sc_id||'',name:item.stock_name||item.name||''};
  }catch{return null;}
}

async function mcPrice(scId){
  // Returns {price, prev} or null
  if(!scId)return null;
  try{
    const url=`https://priceapi.moneycontrol.com/pricefeed/nse/equitycash/${encodeURIComponent(scId)}`;
    const r=await fetch(url,{signal:AbortSignal.timeout(8000)});
    if(!r.ok)return null;
    const d=await r.json();
    const data=d?.data;if(!data)return null;
    const price=parseFloat(data.pricecurrent||0);
    const prev=parseFloat(data.priceprevclose||price||0);
    if(isFinite(price)&&price>0)return{price,prev:isFinite(prev)&&prev>0?prev:price,name:data.SC_FULLNM||''};
  }catch{}
  return null;
}

// MoneyControl combined: ISIN/ticker → live price (one call chain, no proxy)
async function fetchMoneyControlDirect(isin,ticker,name){
  // Try ISIN first (most precise)
  let mc=null;
  if(isin&&/^IN[A-Z0-9]{10}$/.test(isin))mc=await mcSearch(isin);
  // Fallback to ticker
  if(!mc&&ticker&&ticker.length>1&&!/^IN[A-Z0-9]{10}$/.test(ticker))mc=await mcSearch(ticker);
  // Fallback to name
  if(!mc&&name&&name.length>3)mc=await mcSearch(name.split(' ').slice(0,3).join(' '));
  if(!mc||!mc.sc_id)return null;
  const priceData=await mcPrice(mc.sc_id);
  if(!priceData)return null;
  return{price:priceData.price,prev:priceData.prev,source:'MoneyControl',resolvedName:priceData.name||mc.name||''};
}

// ── FALLBACK: Yahoo Finance via CORS proxy ──
async function fetchYahooPrice(ticker){
  if(!ticker||/^IN[A-Z0-9]{10}$/.test(ticker))return null;
  const sym=ticker.toUpperCase()+'.NS';
  const url=`https://query1.finance.yahoo.com/v8/finance/chart/${encodeURIComponent(sym)}?interval=1d&range=2d`;
  try{
    const body=await tryProxies(url,12000);if(!body)return null;
    const d=typeof body==='string'?JSON.parse(body):body;
    const meta=d?.chart?.result?.[0]?.meta;
    if(!meta)return null;
    const price=parseFloat(meta.regularMarketPrice||0);
    const prev=parseFloat(meta.chartPreviousClose||meta.previousClose||price||0);
    if(isFinite(price)&&price>0)return{price,prev:isFinite(prev)&&prev>0?prev:price,source:'Yahoo'};
  }catch{}
  return null;
}

// ── FALLBACK: NSE India via CORS proxy ──
async function fetchNSEprice(sym){
  if(!sym||/^IN[A-Z0-9]{10}$/.test(sym))return null;
  const url=`https://www.nseindia.com/api/quote-equity?symbol=${encodeURIComponent(sym.toUpperCase())}`;
  try{
    const body=await tryProxies(url,12000);if(!body)return null;
    const d=typeof body==='string'?JSON.parse(body):body;
    const price=parseFloat(d?.priceInfo?.lastPrice||d?.priceInfo?.closePrice||0);
    const prev=parseFloat(d?.priceInfo?.previousClose||price||0);
    if(isFinite(price)&&price>0)return{price,prev:isFinite(prev)&&prev>0?prev:price,source:'NSE'};
  }catch{}
  return null;
}

// ── FALLBACK: BSE India via CORS proxy ──
async function fetchBSEprice(isin){
  if(!isin||!/^IN[A-Z0-9]{10}$/.test(isin))return null;
  const url=`https://api.bseindia.com/BseIndiaAPI/api/getScripHeaderData/w?Debtflag=&scripcode=&isin=${isin}&Segmentid=&Series=&isintick=false`;
  try{
    const body=await tryProxies(url,11000);if(!body)return null;
    const d=typeof body==='string'?JSON.parse(body):body;
    const price=parseFloat(d?.CurrRate||d?.Ltp||d?.current_price||0);
    const prev=parseFloat(d?.PrevClose||d?.Cls||price||0);
    if(isFinite(price)&&price>0)return{price,prev:isFinite(prev)&&prev>0?prev:price,source:'BSE'};
  }catch{}
  return null;
}

// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// MASTER fetchStockPrice — MoneyControl FIRST (direct, no proxy)
// Then Yahoo Finance, NSE, BSE as fallbacks via proxy
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
async function fetchStockPrice(ticker,isin,name){
  const cleanISIN=(isin||'').toUpperCase().trim();
  const cleanTicker=(ticker||'').replace(/\.(NS|BO|NSE|BSE)$/i,'').trim().toUpperCase();
  // Resolve ticker from local NSE map if ISIN provided
  let nseSym=cleanTicker;
  if(/^IN[A-Z0-9]{10}$/.test(cleanISIN)){const m=NSE.find(s=>s.isin===cleanISIN);if(m)nseSym=m.t;}
  if(/^IN[A-Z0-9]{10}$/.test(nseSym)){const m=NSE.find(s=>s.isin===nseSym);if(m)nseSym=m.t;else nseSym='';}
  const ts=hhMM();

  // ── PRIMARY: MoneyControl Direct (no proxy, CORS enabled) ──
  const mc=await fetchMoneyControlDirect(cleanISIN,nseSym||cleanTicker,name);
  if(mc&&mc.price>0)return{price:mc.price,prev:mc.prev,ts,source:mc.source};

  // ── FALLBACK 1: Yahoo Finance via proxy ──
  if(nseSym){
    const yf=await fetchYahooPrice(nseSym);
    if(yf&&yf.price>0)return{...yf,ts};
  }

  // ── FALLBACK 2: NSE direct via proxy ──
  if(nseSym){
    const nse=await fetchNSEprice(nseSym);
    if(nse&&nse.price>0)return{...nse,ts};
  }

  // ── FALLBACK 3: BSE via proxy (by ISIN) ──
  if(/^IN[A-Z0-9]{10}$/.test(cleanISIN)){
    const bse=await fetchBSEprice(cleanISIN);
    if(bse&&bse.price>0)return{...bse,ts};
  }

  // ── FALLBACK 4: Try alternate ticker if different from nseSym ──
  if(cleanTicker&&cleanTicker!==nseSym&&!/^IN[A-Z0-9]{10}$/.test(cleanTicker)){
    const mc2=await fetchMoneyControlDirect('',cleanTicker,'');
    if(mc2&&mc2.price>0)return{price:mc2.price,prev:mc2.prev,ts,source:mc2.source};
  }

  return null;
}
function hhMM(){return new Date().toLocaleTimeString('en-IN',{hour:'2-digit',minute:'2-digit'});}

// ── resolveISINOnce: ISIN → {name,ticker,source} ──
async function resolveISINOnce(isin){
  if(!/^IN[A-Z0-9]{10}$/.test(isin||''))return null;
  // 1. Local NSE map (instant)
  const local=NSE.find(s=>s.isin===isin);
  if(local)return{name:local.n,ticker:local.t,source:'NSE-local'};
  // 2. MoneyControl search (direct, no proxy)
  try{
    const mc=await mcSearch(isin);
    if(mc&&mc.sc_id){
      // Extract ticker from the search result link if available
      const ticker=mc.sc_id.toUpperCase();
      return{name:mc.name||'',ticker:ticker,source:'MoneyControl'};
    }
  }catch{}
  // 3. BSE API via proxy
  try{
    const body=await tryProxies(`https://api.bseindia.com/BseIndiaAPI/api/getScripHeaderData/w?Debtflag=&scripcode=&isin=${isin}&Segmentid=&Series=&isintick=false`);
    if(body){
      const d=typeof body==='string'?JSON.parse(body):body;
      const nm=d?.CompanyName||d?.LongName||d?.companyName||'';
      const sm=d?.Symbol||d?.TckrSymb||d?.NSESymbol||'';
      const cleanCo=n=>String(n||'').replace(/&amp;/g,'&').replace(/\s+(?:limited|ltd\.?|pvt\.?|private|corp\.?)\s*$/gi,'').replace(/\s+/g,' ').trim().slice(0,80);
      const cleanTk=t=>String(t||'').replace(/\.(NS|BO|NSE|BSE)$/i,'').replace(/[^A-Z0-9\-&]/gi,'').toUpperCase().slice(0,15);
      if(nm&&nm.length>2)return{name:cleanCo(nm),ticker:sm?cleanTk(sm):'',source:'BSE'};
    }
  }catch{}
  return null;
}
</script>



<script>
// MF MODAL
function openAddFund(){
  editMFi=null;selFund=null;
  g('mf-mt').textContent='Add Mutual Fund';
  ['mf-q','mf-amfi','mf-isin','mf-units','mf-avgn','mf-sip','mf-note'].forEach(id=>{const el=g(id);if(el)el.value='';});
  const dt=g('mf-date');if(dt)dt.valueAsDate=new Date();
  const sd=g('mf-sd');if(sd)sd.classList.remove('open');
  const sb=g('mf-sb');if(sb)sb.style.display='none';
  const sv=g('mf-save');if(sv){sv.disabled=true;sv.textContent='Save Fund';}
  const pv=g('mf-prev');if(pv)pv.style.display='none';
  openOv('ov-fund');setTimeout(()=>{const q=g('mf-q');if(q)q.focus();},120);
}
function editMF(i){
  editMFi=i;const f=cm().holdings[i];if(!f)return;
  selFund={schemeCode:f.amfiCode,schemeName:f.name,isin:f.isin||''};
  g('mf-mt').textContent='Edit Fund';g('mf-q').value=f.name;g('mf-units').value=f.units;
  g('mf-amfi').value=f.amfiCode||'';g('mf-isin').value=f.isin||'';
  g('mf-avgn').value=f.avgNav||0;g('mf-sip').value=f.sip||'';g('mf-note').value=f.note||'';g('mf-date').value=f.buyDate||'';
  g('mf-sd').classList.remove('open');g('mf-sb').style.display='block';g('mf-sb-n').textContent=f.name;g('mf-sb-c').textContent='AMFI: '+(f.amfiCode||'—')+(f.isin?' · ISIN: '+f.isin:'');
  g('mf-save').disabled=false;g('mf-save').textContent='Update Fund';showMFP();openOv('ov-fund');
}
function showMFP(){
  const u=sf(g('mf-units').value),a=sf(g('mf-avgn').value),p=g('mf-prev');if(!p)return;
  if(u>0){p.style.display='block';p.innerHTML=a>0?`<strong>Preview:</strong> ${fm(u,4)} units × <span class="ru">ரூ</span>${fm(a,4)} = <strong style="color:var(--ind)"><span class="ru">ரூ</span>${fm(u*a,2)} invested</strong>`:`<strong>Preview:</strong> ${fm(u,4)} units · avg NAV = <span class="ru">ரூ</span>0`;}
  else{p.style.display='none';}
}
function debMF(){clearTimeout(mfDebT);mfDebT=setTimeout(doMFSearch,280);}
async function doMFSearch(){
  const q=(g('mf-q').value||'').trim();const drop=g('mf-sd');if(!drop)return;
  if(q.length<3){drop.classList.remove('open');return;}
  drop.classList.add('open');
  // Direct AMFI code lookup (4-7 digit number)
  if(/^\d{4,7}$/.test(q)){
    drop.innerHTML='<div class="si"><div class="si-n ts">Looking up AMFI code…</div></div>';
    try{
      const r=await fetch(`https://api.mfapi.in/mf/${q}`,{signal:AbortSignal.timeout(8000)});
      if(r.ok){const d=await r.json();const nm=d?.meta?.scheme_name;if(nm){const isinG=d?.meta?.isin_growth||d?.meta?.isinGrowth||'';drop.innerHTML=`<div class="si" onclick='pickMF(${JSON.stringify({schemeCode:q,schemeName:nm,isinGrowth:isinG}).replace(/'/g,"&#39;")})'><div class="si-n">${escH(nm)}</div><div class="si-m">AMFI: ${q}${isinG?' · '+isinG:''}</div></div>`;return;}}
    }catch{}
    drop.innerHTML='<div class="si"><div class="si-n ts">No match.</div></div>';return;
  }
  drop.innerHTML='<div class="si"><div class="si-n ts">Searching AMFI…</div></div>';
  try{
    const r=await fetch(`https://api.mfapi.in/mf/search?q=${encodeURIComponent(q)}`,{signal:AbortSignal.timeout(9000)});
    const rs=await r.json();
    if(!Array.isArray(rs)||!rs.length){drop.innerHTML='<div class="si"><div class="si-n ts">No results.</div></div>';return;}
    drop.innerHTML=rs.slice(0,14).map(x=>`<div class="si" onclick='pickMF(${JSON.stringify(x).replace(/'/g,"&#39;")})'><div class="si-n">${escH(x.schemeName)}</div><div class="si-m">AMFI: ${x.schemeCode}${x.isinGrowth?' · '+x.isinGrowth:''}</div></div>`).join('');
  }catch{drop.innerHTML='<div class="si"><div class="si-n" style="color:var(--rose)">Search failed — check internet.</div></div>';}
}
function pickMF(f){
  selFund=f;
  if(f.isinGrowth)selFund.isin=f.isinGrowth;
  else if(f.isinDividend)selFund.isin=f.isinDividend;
  g('mf-q').value=f.schemeName;
  g('mf-amfi').value=f.schemeCode;
  if(selFund.isin)g('mf-isin').value=selFund.isin;
  g('mf-sd').classList.remove('open');
  g('mf-sb').style.display='block';
  g('mf-sb-n').textContent=f.schemeName;
  g('mf-sb-c').textContent='AMFI: '+f.schemeCode+(selFund.isin?' · ISIN: '+selFund.isin:'');
  g('mf-save').disabled=false;
  const uEl=g('mf-units');if(uEl)uEl.focus();
}
let _mfAmfiTimer=null;
function onMFAmfiChange(){
  clearTimeout(_mfAmfiTimer);
  _mfAmfiTimer=setTimeout(async()=>{
    const code=(g('mf-amfi').value||'').trim();
    if(!/^\d{4,7}$/.test(code))return;
    try{
      const r=await fetch(`https://api.mfapi.in/mf/${code}`,{signal:AbortSignal.timeout(8000)});
      if(!r.ok)return;const d=await r.json();const nm=d?.meta?.scheme_name;if(!nm)return;
      const isinG=d?.meta?.isin_growth||d?.meta?.isinGrowth||'';
      selFund={schemeCode:code,schemeName:nm,isin:isinG};
      g('mf-q').value=nm;
      if(isinG&&!g('mf-isin').value)g('mf-isin').value=isinG;
      g('mf-sb').style.display='block';g('mf-sb-n').textContent=nm;
      g('mf-sb-c').textContent='AMFI: '+code+(isinG?' · ISIN: '+isinG:'')+' [auto-resolved]';
      g('mf-save').disabled=false;
    }catch{}
  },350);
}
async function saveFund(){
  // AMFI is MANDATORY. Try to resolve from manual amfi field, selFund, or ISIN
  let amfi=(g('mf-amfi').value||'').trim();
  let isin=(g('mf-isin').value||'').trim().toUpperCase();
  const units=sf(g('mf-units').value),avgN=sf(g('mf-avgn').value,0);
  if(units<=0){toast('Enter valid units','err');return;}
  const btn=g('mf-save');btn.disabled=true;btn.textContent='Resolving via AMFI…';
  try{
    let canonicalName='';
    // If no AMFI but ISIN present, resolve via AMFI search
    if(!amfi&&/^IN[A-Z0-9]{10}$/.test(isin)){
      try{
        const r=await fetch(`https://api.mfapi.in/mf/search?q=${encodeURIComponent(isin)}`,{signal:AbortSignal.timeout(9000)});
        const rs=await r.json();
        if(Array.isArray(rs)&&rs.length){
          const m=rs.find(x=>x.isinGrowth===isin||x.isinDividend===isin)||rs.find(x=>{const n=(x.schemeName||'').toUpperCase();return n.includes('DIRECT')&&(n.includes('GROWTH')||n.includes(' GR '));})||rs[0];
          if(m){amfi=String(m.schemeCode);canonicalName=m.schemeName||'';if(!isin&&m.isinGrowth)isin=m.isinGrowth;}
        }
      }catch{}
    }
    if(!amfi&&selFund?.schemeCode)amfi=String(selFund.schemeCode);
    if(!amfi){btn.disabled=false;btn.textContent=editMFi!==null?'Update Fund':'Save Fund';toast('AMFI Code is mandatory — search by name or enter AMFI code / ISIN','err');return;}
    if(!/^\d{3,8}$/.test(amfi)){btn.disabled=false;btn.textContent=editMFi!==null?'Update Fund':'Save Fund';toast('AMFI Code must be numeric','err');return;}
    // Fetch canonical name from AMFI if not already resolved
    if(!canonicalName){
      try{
        const r=await fetch(`https://api.mfapi.in/mf/${amfi}`,{signal:AbortSignal.timeout(8000)});
        if(r.ok){const d=await r.json();canonicalName=d?.meta?.scheme_name||'';if(!isin)isin=d?.meta?.isin_growth||d?.meta?.isinGrowth||'';}
      }catch{}
    }
    if(!canonicalName)canonicalName=selFund?.schemeName||(g('mf-q').value||'').trim();
    if(!canonicalName){btn.disabled=false;btn.textContent=editMFi!==null?'Update Fund':'Save Fund';toast('Could not resolve fund name — verify AMFI code','err');return;}
    const nd=await fetchNAV(amfi);
    let currentNav=avgN>0?avgN:0,prevNav=avgN>0?avgN:0,navDate='',navCat='';
    if(nd&&nd.nav>0){currentNav=nd.nav;prevNav=nd.prev||nd.nav;navDate=nd.date||'';navCat=nd.cat||'';}
    const entry={
      name:canonicalName,amfiCode:amfi,
      isin:/^IN[A-Z0-9]{10}$/.test(isin)?isin:'',
      units,avgNav:avgN,currentNav,prevNav,navDate,
      category:navCat,folio:'',
      marketVal:units*currentNav,costVal:units*avgN,
      sip:sf(g('mf-sip').value),
      buyDate:g('mf-date').value||'',
      note:g('mf-note').value||'',
      addedAt:new Date().toISOString()
    };
    const m=cm();
    if(editMFi!==null){entry.addedAt=m.holdings[editMFi]?.addedAt||entry.addedAt;m.holdings[editMFi]=entry;}
    else m.holdings.push(entry);
    persist();renderAll();closeOv('ov-fund');
    const navMsg=currentNav>0?` · NAV: ${RU}${fm(currentNav,4)}`:'';
    toast((editMFi!==null?'✓ Fund updated':'✓ Fund added')+navMsg+' [AMFI]','ok');
  }catch(e){btn.disabled=false;btn.textContent=editMFi!==null?'Update Fund':'Save Fund';toast('Error: '+e.message,'err');}
}

  const dt=g('stk-date');if(dt)dt.valueAsDate=new Date();
  g('stk-sd').classList.remove('open');g('stk-sb').style.display='none';g('stk-save').disabled=true;
  const pv=g('stk-prev');if(pv)pv.style.display='none';

}

  selStock={ticker:s.ticker,name:s.name||s.ticker,isin:s.isin||''};
  g('stk-mt').textContent='Edit Stock';g('stk-q').value=s.name||s.ticker;g('stk-qty').value=s.qty;g('stk-avg').value=s.avgPrice||0;
  g('stk-isin').value=s.isin||'';g('stk-date').value=s.buyDate||'';g('stk-note').value=s.note||'';

}
function showStkP(){const q=sf(g('stk-qty').value),a=sf(g('stk-avg').value),p=g('stk-prev');if(!p)return;if(q>0){p.style.display='block';p.innerHTML=a>0?`<strong>Preview:</strong> ${q} × <span class="ru">ரூ</span>${fm(a,2)} = <strong style="color:var(--ind)"><span class="ru">ரூ</span>${fm(q*a,2)} invested</strong>`:`<strong>Preview:</strong> ${q} shares · avg = <span class="ru">ரூ</span>0`;}else{p.style.display='none';}}
function debStk(){clearTimeout(stkDebT);stkDebT=setTimeout(doStkSearch,130);}
let _stkIsinTimer=null;
function onStkIsinChange(){
  clearTimeout(_stkIsinTimer);
  _stkIsinTimer=setTimeout(async()=>{
    const isin=(g('stk-isin').value||'').trim().toUpperCase();
    if(!/^IN[A-Z0-9]{10}$/.test(isin))return;
    // 1. Local NSE array lookup (instant)
    const local=NSE.find(s=>s.isin===isin);
    if(local){
      selStock={ticker:local.t,name:local.n,isin:local.isin};
      g('stk-q').value=local.n;
      g('stk-sd').classList.remove('open');
      g('stk-sb').style.display='block';
      g('stk-sb-n').textContent=local.n;
      g('stk-sb-c').textContent=local.t+' · '+local.isin+' · NSE [auto-resolved]';
      g('stk-save').disabled=false;
      return;
    }
    // 2. MoneyControl search by ISIN (direct, no proxy)
    g('stk-sb').style.display='block';
    g('stk-sb-n').textContent='Resolving ISIN '+isin+'…';
    g('stk-sb-c').textContent='Searching MoneyControl…';
    try{
      const mc=await mcSearch(isin);
      if(mc&&mc.sc_id){
        selStock={ticker:mc.sc_id.toUpperCase(),name:mc.name||isin,isin:isin};
        g('stk-q').value=mc.name||isin;
        g('stk-sd').classList.remove('open');
        g('stk-sb-n').textContent=mc.name||isin;
        g('stk-sb-c').textContent=mc.sc_id.toUpperCase()+' · '+isin+' · MoneyControl [auto-resolved]';
        g('stk-save').disabled=false;
        return;
      }
    }catch{}
    // 3. Fallback: allow using ISIN as-is
    selStock={ticker:isin,name:isin,isin:isin};
    g('stk-q').value=isin;
    g('stk-sb-n').textContent=isin+' (ISIN)';
    g('stk-sb-c').textContent='Will resolve name on save · live price via MoneyControl';
    g('stk-save').disabled=false;
  },400);
}
async function doStkSearch(){
  const q=(g('stk-q').value||'').trim();const drop=g('stk-sd');if(!drop)return;
  if(q.length<1){drop.classList.remove('open');return;}
  const qu=q.toUpperCase();
  drop.classList.add('open');
  // Full ISIN entered → live resolution
  if(/^IN[A-Z0-9]{10}$/.test(qu)){
    const local=NSE.find(s=>s.isin===qu);
    if(local){drop.innerHTML=`<div class="si" onclick='pickStk(${JSON.stringify(local).replace(/'/g,"&#39;")})'><div class="si-n">${escH(local.n)}</div><div class="si-m">${local.t} · ${local.isin} · NSE (local)</div></div>`;return;}
    drop.innerHTML='<div class="si"><div class="si-n ts">Resolving ISIN '+qu+' via MoneyControl…</div></div>';
    try{
      const r=await resolveISINOnce(qu);
      if(r&&(r.name||r.ticker)){
        const stk={n:r.name||qu,t:r.ticker||qu,isin:qu};
        drop.innerHTML=`<div class="si" onclick='pickStk(${JSON.stringify(stk).replace(/'/g,"&#39;")})'><div class="si-n">${escH(stk.n)}</div><div class="si-m">${stk.t} · ${qu} · ${r.source}</div></div>`
          +`<div class="si si-custom" style="border-top:1px solid var(--bdr2)" onclick="addCustomTicker('${qu}')"><div class="si-n">+ Use ISIN ${qu} as-is</div><div class="si-m">Live price resolves on save</div></div>`;
        return;
      }
    }catch{}
    drop.innerHTML=`<div class="si si-custom" onclick="addCustomTicker('${qu}')"><div class="si-n">+ Use ${qu} as ISIN (live on save)</div><div class="si-m">No name match — will retry on save</div></div>`;
    return;
  }
  // Name/ticker search in local NSE list
  const isPartialISIN=/^IN[A-Z0-9]{0,11}$/.test(qu)&&qu.length>=4;
  const hits=NSE.filter(s=>(isPartialISIN?(s.isin&&s.isin.startsWith(qu)):false)||s.t.startsWith(qu)||s.n.toUpperCase().includes(qu)||(s.isin&&s.isin.includes(qu))).slice(0,14);
  let html=hits.map(x=>`<div class="si" onclick='pickStk(${JSON.stringify(x).replace(/'/g,"&#39;")})'><div class="si-n">${escH(x.n)}</div><div class="si-m">${x.t} · ${x.isin} · NSE</div></div>`).join('');
  html+=`<div class="si si-custom" style="border-top:1px solid var(--bdr2)" onclick="addCustomTicker('${qu.replace(/['"<>]/g,'')}')"><div class="si-n">+ Use "${escH(q)}" as ticker</div><div class="si-m">Any NSE/BSE ticker · ISIN resolves live</div></div>`;
  drop.innerHTML=html;
}
function pickStk(s){selStock={ticker:s.t,name:s.n,isin:s.isin||''};g('stk-q').value=s.n;g('stk-isin').value=s.isin||'';g('stk-sd').classList.remove('open');g('stk-sb').style.display='block';g('stk-sb-n').textContent=s.n;g('stk-sb-c').textContent=`${s.t} · ${s.isin||'—'} · NSE`;g('stk-save').disabled=false;const qEl=g('stk-qty');if(qEl)qEl.focus();}
function addCustomTicker(t){
  if(!t)return;
  const isISIN=/^IN[A-Z0-9]{10}$/.test(t);
  if(isISIN){selStock={ticker:t,name:t,isin:t};g('stk-q').value=t;g('stk-isin').value=t;}
  else{selStock={ticker:t,name:t,isin:''};g('stk-q').value=t;}
  g('stk-sd').classList.remove('open');g('stk-sb').style.display='block';
  g('stk-sb-n').textContent=t+(isISIN?' (ISIN)':' (Ticker)');
  g('stk-sb-c').textContent=isISIN?'ISIN → live resolution on save (NSE/BSE/Groww/Tickertape/MoneyControl)':'NSE/BSE/Screener.in';
  g('stk-save').disabled=false;const qEl=g('stk-qty');if(qEl)qEl.focus();
}
async function saveStock(){
  if(!selStock){toast('Select or enter a stock first','err');return;}
  const qty=sf(g('stk-qty').value),avg=sf(g('stk-avg').value,0);
  if(qty<=0){toast('Enter valid quantity','err');return;}

  // ISIN: clean from field or selStock
  const rawISIN=((g('stk-isin').value||selStock.isin||'')).toUpperCase().replace(/[^A-Z0-9]/g,'').trim();
  const isin=/^IN[A-Z0-9]{10}$/.test(rawISIN)?rawISIN:'';

  let resolvedName=selStock.name||selStock.ticker||'';
  let resolvedTicker=(selStock.ticker||'').replace(/\.(NS|BO|NSE|BSE)$/i,'').trim().toUpperCase();

  // Step 1: NSE local map by ISIN (instant)
  if(isin){const m=NSE.find(s=>s.isin===isin);if(m){resolvedName=m.n;resolvedTicker=m.t;}}
  // Step 2: ticker is ISIN-shaped → look up NSE map
  if(/^IN[A-Z0-9]{10}$/.test(resolvedTicker)){const m=NSE.find(s=>s.isin===resolvedTicker);if(m){resolvedName=m.n;resolvedTicker=m.t;}}

  // Step 3: live ISIN resolution if name/ticker still looks like ISIN or is too short
  const needsLiveResolve=isin&&(!resolvedName||resolvedName.length<=2||/^IN[A-Z0-9]{10}$/.test(resolvedName)||resolvedName===isin||!resolvedTicker||/^IN[A-Z0-9]{10}$/.test(resolvedTicker));
  if(needsLiveResolve){
    const sb=g('stk-sb');if(sb){g('stk-sb-n').textContent='Resolving ISIN '+isin+'…';g('stk-sb-c').textContent='BSE / Groww / Tickertape / MoneyControl';}
    const r=await resolveISINOnce(isin);
    if(r){if(r.name&&r.name.length>2&&!/^IN[A-Z0-9]{10}$/.test(r.name))resolvedName=r.name;if(r.ticker&&r.ticker.length>0&&!/^IN[A-Z0-9]{10}$/.test(r.ticker))resolvedTicker=r.ticker;}
  }

  // Step 4: final fallback — use ISIN as ticker if nothing resolved
  if(!resolvedTicker||/^IN[A-Z0-9]{10}$/.test(resolvedTicker))resolvedTicker=isin||(g('stk-q').value||'').trim().toUpperCase().replace(/[^A-Z0-9\-&]/g,'').slice(0,12);
  if(!resolvedTicker){toast('Could not resolve ticker — enter a valid ISIN or NSE ticker','err');return;}
  if(!resolvedName||resolvedName.length<2)resolvedName=resolvedTicker;

  const entry={ticker:resolvedTicker,name:resolvedName,exchange:'NS',isin,qty,avgPrice:avg,currentPrice:avg,prevPrice:avg,liveOk:false,lastFetch:'',priceSource:null,buyDate:g('stk-date').value||'',note:g('stk-note').value||'',addedAt:new Date().toISOString()};
  const m=cm();
  if(editSTi!==null){entry.addedAt=m.stocks[editSTi]?.addedAt||entry.addedAt;m.stocks[editSTi]=entry;}
  else m.stocks.push(entry);
  persist();closeOv('ov-stock');renderAll();toast('✓ Stock saved — fetching live price…','ok');
  const idx=editSTi!==null?editSTi:m.stocks.length-1;

  // Fetch price using ISIN-first chain
  const r=await fetchStockPrice(resolvedTicker,isin,resolvedName);
  if(r&&r.price>0&&m.stocks[idx]){
    m.stocks[idx].currentPrice=r.price;m.stocks[idx].prevPrice=r.prev||r.price;
    m.stocks[idx].lastFetch=hhMM();m.stocks[idx].liveOk=true;m.stocks[idx].priceSource=r.source;
    persist();renderAll();toast(`✓ ${resolvedName}: ${RU}${fm(r.price,2)} [${r.source}]`,'ok');
  }else toast('Live price pending — tap ↻ Live Prices to retry','info');
}
</script>

<script>
// RENDER BANKS
function renderBanks(){
  const accts=cm().bankAccounts||[],today=new Date();
  let depTotal=0,loanTotal=0,emiTotal=0,active=0;
  for(const a of accts){
    if(a.atype==='loan'){loanTotal+=sf(a.loanBal);emiTotal+=sf(a.emi);}
    else if(['rd','fd'].includes(a.atype))depTotal+=sf(a.depAmt);
    active++;
  }
  g('bnk-dep-total').innerHTML=`<span class="ru">ரூ</span>${fL(depTotal).replace(RU,'')}`;
  g('bnk-cnt').textContent=`${accts.length} account${accts.length!==1?'s':''}`;
  g('bnk-loan-total').innerHTML=`<span class="ru">ரூ</span>${fL(loanTotal).replace(RU,'')}`;
  g('bnk-emi-total').innerHTML=`<span class="ru">ரூ</span>${fL(emiTotal).replace(RU,'')}`;
  g('bnk-active-cnt').textContent=active;

  let html=accts.map((a,i)=>{
    const tc=BANK_COL[a.atype]||'var(--tx3)';
    const isLoan=a.atype==='loan';
    const isFDRD=['rd','fd'].includes(a.atype);
    const isDemat=a.atype==='demat';
    const accDisplay=a.accno?(a.atype==='demat'?a.dematNo||a.accno:a.accno):'—';
    const maskedAcc=accDisplay&&accDisplay.length>4?'••••'+accDisplay.slice(-4):accDisplay;
    return`<div class="bnk-c at-${a.atype||'savings'}">
      <div class="bnk-name">${escH(a.holder)}</div>
      <span class="bnk-type" style="background:${tc}22;color:${tc}">${BANK_LBL[a.atype]||'Account'}</span>
      ${isLoan?`<span class="loan-tag">${escH(a.loanType||'Loan')}</span>`:''}
      <div class="bnk-row"><span class="bnk-rl">Bank / Institution</span><span class="bnk-rv">${escH(a.bank||'—')}</span></div>
      <div class="bnk-row"><span class="bnk-rl">Account No.</span><span class="bnk-rv" style="font-family:'JetBrains Mono',monospace;font-size:10px">${escH(maskedAcc)}</span></div>
      ${isLoan?`<div class="bnk-row"><span class="bnk-rl">Outstanding</span><span class="bnk-rv" style="color:var(--rose);font-weight:700">${fL(a.loanBal)}</span></div><div class="bnk-row"><span class="bnk-rl">EMI / Month</span><span class="bnk-rv">${fL(a.emi)}</span></div><div class="bnk-row"><span class="bnk-rl">ROI</span><span class="bnk-rv">${a.roi?fm(a.roi,2)+'%':'—'}</span></div>`:''}
      ${isFDRD?`<div class="bnk-row"><span class="bnk-rl">Deposit</span><span class="bnk-rv" style="color:var(--ind);font-weight:700">${fL(a.depAmt)}</span></div><div class="bnk-row"><span class="bnk-rl">Maturity</span><span class="bnk-rv">${a.depEnd||'—'}</span></div>`:''}
      ${isDemat?`<div class="bnk-row"><span class="bnk-rl">Depository</span><span class="bnk-rv">${escH(a.depository||'—')}</span></div>`:''}
      ${!isLoan&&!isFDRD&&!isDemat?`<div class="bnk-row"><span class="bnk-rl">IFSC</span><span class="bnk-rv" style="font-family:'JetBrains Mono',monospace;font-size:10px">${escH(a.ifsc||'—')}</span></div>`:''}
      <div class="bnk-actions">
        <button class="bka" onclick="editBank(${i})">Edit</button>
        <button class="bka" style="color:var(--rose);flex:.4" onclick="delBank(${i})">✕</button>
      </div>
    </div>`;
  }).join('');
  html+=`<div class="bnk-c add-bnk" onclick="openAddBank()"><div style="font-size:24px;color:var(--tx3)">+</div><div style="font-size:11.5px;font-weight:700;color:var(--tx2)">Add Account</div></div>`;
  g('bank-grid').innerHTML=html;
}
</script>


<script>
// PDF.js LOADER
async function ensurePDFJS(){
  if(typeof pdfjsLib!=='undefined'){if(!pdfjsLib.GlobalWorkerOptions.workerSrc)pdfjsLib.GlobalWorkerOptions.workerSrc='https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/pdf.js/3.11.174/pdf.worker.min.js';return true;}
  try{
    await new Promise((res,rej)=>{const s=document.createElement('script');s.src='https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/pdf.js/3.11.174/pdf.min.js';s.onload=res;s.onerror=rej;document.head.appendChild(s);});
    pdfjsLib.GlobalWorkerOptions.workerSrc='https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/pdf.js/3.11.174/pdf.worker.min.js';return true;
  }catch{return false;}
}
async function extractPDFText(file,password){
  const ok=await ensurePDFJS();if(!ok)throw new Error('PDF.js failed to load. Use TXT format instead.');
  const ab=await file.arrayBuffer();const params={data:new Uint8Array(ab),useSystemFonts:true};
  if(password)params.password=password;
  let pdf;
  try{pdf=await pdfjsLib.getDocument(params).promise;}
  catch(err){if(err?.name==='PasswordException'||err?.code===1||String(err).toLowerCase().includes('password'))throw Object.assign(new Error('PDF_PWD'),{isPwd:true});throw err;}
  let out='';
  // Reconstruct lines using Y-coordinate of each text item so that the parser
  // sees one row per visual line (PDF.js text items are not pre-joined into lines).
  for(let i=1;i<=pdf.numPages;i++){
    const pg=await pdf.getPage(i);const c=await pg.getTextContent();
    const rows=new Map();
    for(const it of c.items){
      if(!it||typeof it.str!=='string')continue;
      const y=it.transform?Math.round(it.transform[5]):0;
      const x=it.transform?it.transform[4]:0;
      if(!rows.has(y))rows.set(y,[]);
      rows.get(y).push({x,s:it.str});
    }
    const ys=[...rows.keys()].sort((a,b)=>b-a);
    const pageLines=[];
    for(const y of ys){
      const items=rows.get(y).sort((a,b)=>a.x-b.x);
      const line=items.map(it=>it.s).join(' ').replace(/\s{2,}/g,' ').trim();
      if(line)pageLines.push(line);
    }
    out+=pageLines.join('\n')+'\n';
  }
  return out;
}

// HANDLE DROPS
function handleDrop(e,type){
  const f=e.dataTransfer?.files?.[0];if(!f)return;
  if(type==='cas')parseCASFile(f);
  else if(type==='demat')parseDematFile(f);
  else if(type==='broker')parseBrokerFile(f);
  else if(type==='bonds')parseBondsFile(f);
  else if(type==='bank')parseBankFile(f);
  else if(type==='ins')parseInsFile(f);
}
function handleCASUpload(e){const f=e.target.files?.[0];if(f)parseCASFile(f);e.target.value='';}
function retryCAS(){if(!pendingCAS)return;const pwd=(g('cas-pwd').value||'').trim();if(!pwd){toast('Enter PDF password','err');return;}parseCASFile(pendingCAS,pwd);}
</script>


<script>
// CAS UPLOAD & PARSER (improved multi-strategy)
async function parseCASFile(file,password){
  pendingCAS=file;const out=g('cas-pout');
  out.style.display='block';out.className='pout inf';out.textContent='Reading file…';
  g('cas-pwd-row').classList.remove('show');
  try{
    let text='';
    if(file.name.toLowerCase().endsWith('.pdf')){
      out.textContent='Extracting PDF text…';
      try{text=await extractPDFText(file,password);}
      catch(err){if(err.isPwd){out.className='pout err';out.innerHTML='🔒 Password-protected PDF. Enter password below.<br><small>CAMS: PAN in UPPERCASE · KFintech: DOB DDMMYYYY</small>';g('cas-pwd-row').classList.add('show');return;}throw err;}
      if(text.trim().length<40){out.className='pout err';out.innerHTML='⚠ No readable text from PDF. Use <strong>MF Central → Detailed CAS → Download as Text (TXT)</strong>.';return;}
    }else if(file.name.match(/\.xlsx?$/i)){text=await xlsxToCSV(file);}
    else{text=await file.text();}
    out.textContent='Parsing Portfolio Summary…';
    const funds=await parseCASPortfolioSummary(text);
    if(!funds.length){
      out.className='pout err';
      out.innerHTML='⚠ No fund data found.<br><br><strong>Tips:</strong><br>• Use <strong>Detailed CAS</strong> (not Simple/Summary-only)<br>• Download as <strong>TXT</strong> from MF Central, CAMS or KFintech<br>• CAMS PDF password = PAN (e.g. ABCDE1234F)<br>• KFintech PDF password = DOB DDMMYYYY';return;
    }
    const m=cm();let added=0,updated=0;
    for(const f of funds){
      const dup=m.holdings.find(h=>(f.amfiCode&&h.amfiCode===f.amfiCode)||h.name.toLowerCase().trim()===f.name.toLowerCase().trim());
      if(!dup){m.holdings.push(f);added++;}
      else{
        // Only update AMFI-verifiable fields, never overwrite user/statement data
        if(f.amfiCode)dup.amfiCode=f.amfiCode;
        if(f.isin&&!dup.isin)dup.isin=f.isin;
        if(f.name&&f.amfiCode)dup.name=f.name;
        if(f.units>0)dup.units=f.units;
        if(f.currentNav>0){dup.currentNav=f.currentNav;dup.navDate=f.navDate||dup.navDate;}
        if(f.folio&&!dup.folio)dup.folio=f.folio;
        if(f.buyDate)dup.buyDate=f.buyDate;
        updated++;
      }
    }
    persist();renderAll();g('cas-pwd-row').classList.remove('show');
    out.className='pout ok';
    out.textContent=`✓ Parsed ${funds.length} fund${funds.length!==1?'s':''}. Added ${added} new${updated?`, updated ${updated} existing`:''}.`;
    if(added>0){out.textContent+=' Refreshing NAVs from AMFI…';setTimeout(()=>refreshAll(true),800);}
  }catch(err){out.className='pout err';out.textContent='Error: '+(err.message||String(err));}
}

async function parseCASPortfolioSummary(raw){
  /* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
     CAS PARSER v4 — MOST-RECENT-WINS, ISIN/AMFI mandatory
     Extracts: Folio, PAN, Closing Unit Balance (most recent),
               NAV on Date (most recent), Total Cost Value,
               ISIN (mandatory), AMFI Code (mandatory via API)
     Sources: MF Central TXT, CAMS TXT/PDF, KFintech TXT/PDF, CSV/XLSX
     Fix: multiple Closing Balance lines → Map.set overwrite → last wins
  ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */
  const funds=[], seen=new Set();
  const num=s=>parseFloat((s||'').replace(/[₹,\s\u20B9]/g,'').replace(/^[\-–]$/,'0'));

  // Normalise
  const text=raw
    .replace(/\r\n/g,'\n').replace(/\r/g,'\n')
    .replace(/[""]/g,'"').replace(/['']/g,"'")
    .replace(/\u00a0/g,' ').replace(/\t/g,' ');
  const lines=text.split('\n').map(l=>l.trim()).filter(Boolean);

  /* ── helper: most recent date from a context string ── */
  function latestDate(ctx){
    const all=ctx.match(/\b(\d{2}[-\/][A-Za-z]{3}[-\/]\d{4}|\d{4}[-\/]\d{2}[-\/]\d{2}|\d{2}[-\/]\d{2}[-\/]\d{4})\b/g)||[];
    return all.sort().reverse()[0]||'';
  }

  /* ── helper: extract ISIN from text ── */
  function extractISIN(ctx){
    const m=ctx.match(/\b(IN[A-Z0-9]{10})\b/);
    return m?m[1]:'';
  }

  /* ── helper: is this line a known header/junk ── */
  function isJunk(l){
    return l.length<5
      ||/^[\-=*#_+]{3,}$/.test(l)
      ||/^[\d\s₹,.%()→:=\-\/]+$/.test(l)
      ||/^\d{2}[-\/]\d{2}[-\/]\d{2,4}/.test(l)
      ||/^\s*(folio|pan|mobile|email|period|page|statement|investor|registrar|amc|dear|plan|option|mode|nominee|kyc|grand\s+total|sub.?total|opening\s+balance|transaction\s+details?|account\s+details?|address|agent|branch|dividend|switch|redemption|load|entry\s+load|exit\s+load|nil|acknowledgement|mutual\s+fund|amfi\s+reg|sebi|rta|total\s+portfolio)\b/i.test(l);
  }


  /* ── STRATEGY A: Folio-block parser (CAMS / KFintech / MF Central TXT) ──
     MOST-RECENT-WINS via Map.set overwrite:
       Same scheme may have Opening Balance + multiple Closing Balance rows.
       Each Closing Balance row overwrites the Map entry → last = most recent.
     Extracts: Folio, PAN, ISIN, Units, NAV, Cost Value, Market Value, Date ── */
  const fundMap=new Map(); // key → data object (overwritten on each Closing Balance)
  let curFolio='', curPAN='', curSchemeName='', curISIN='', inScheme=false;

  // Document-level PAN as fallback
  const headerPanM=text.match(/\bPAN\s*(?:no\.?|number)?\s*[:\-]?\s*([A-Z]{5}[0-9]{4}[A-Z])\b/i);
  if(headerPanM)curPAN=headerPanM[1];

  for(let i=0;i<lines.length;i++){
    const l=lines[i];

    // Detect folio header — grab PAN from same line or next line
    const folioM=l.match(/folio\s*(?:no\.?|number|#)?\s*[:\-]?\s*([A-Z0-9\/\-]{4,20})/i);
    if(folioM){
      curFolio=folioM[1].trim();inScheme=false;
      const panInline=l.match(/\b([A-Z]{5}[0-9]{4}[A-Z])\b/);
      if(panInline)curPAN=panInline[1];
      else{const panNext=(lines[i+1]||'').match(/\b([A-Z]{5}[0-9]{4}[A-Z])\b/);if(panNext)curPAN=panNext[1];}
      continue;
    }

    // Standalone PAN line
    const panLineM=l.match(/\bPAN\s*[:\-]?\s*([A-Z]{5}[0-9]{4}[A-Z])\b/i);
    if(panLineM)curPAN=panLineM[1];

    // ISIN standalone line
    const isinLineM=l.match(/^\s*ISIN\s*[:\-]?\s*(IN[A-Z0-9]{10})/i);
    if(isinLineM){curISIN=isinLineM[1];continue;}

    // Scheme name detection: has ISIN nearby OR is a known fund keyword line
    const nextCtx=(lines[i+1]||'')+(lines[i+2]||'');
    const hasISINNearby=/\bIN[A-Z0-9]{10}\b/.test(l+' '+nextCtx);
    if(!isJunk(l)&&(hasISINNearby||/fund|direct|growth|regular|scheme|plan|nifty|sensex|index|flexi|mid|small|large|elss|gilt|liquid|debt|hybrid|balanced|equity|bluechip|focused|value|multi|gold|silver|intl|global|pharma|fmcg|infra|banking|tech|nasdaq/i.test(l))&&l.length>10){
      const lineISIN=extractISIN(l);
      curSchemeName=l.replace(/ISIN\s*[:\-]?\s*IN[A-Z0-9]{10}/gi,'').replace(/\s{2,}/g,' ').trim();
      if(lineISIN)curISIN=lineISIN;
      inScheme=true;
      continue;
    }

    // Closing Balance / Closing Unit Balance line → MOST-RECENT-WINS via Map.set
    if(inScheme&&/closing\s+(?:unit\s+)?bal(?:ance)?/i.test(l)){
      const nums=(l.match(/[\d,]+\.?\d*/g)||[]).map(x=>parseFloat(x.replace(/,/g,''))).filter(n=>isFinite(n)&&n>=0);
      let units=0,navVal=0,costVal=0,marketVal=0;
      if(nums.length>=4){units=nums[0];navVal=nums[1];costVal=nums[2];marketVal=nums[3];}
      else if(nums.length===3){units=nums[0];costVal=nums[1];marketVal=nums[2];}
      else if(nums.length===2){units=nums[0];marketVal=nums[1];}
      else if(nums.length===1){units=nums[0];}
      if(units<=0||units>1e8)continue;
      if(navVal<=0&&marketVal>0&&units>0)navVal=+(marketVal/units).toFixed(4);
      const avgNav=costVal>0&&units>0?+(costVal/units).toFixed(4):0;
      // NAV date: look for date on same line or inline
      const dateInLine=(l.match(/\b(\d{1,2}[-\/][A-Za-z]{3}[-\/]\d{4}|\d{4}[-\/]\d{2}[-\/]\d{2}|\d{1,2}[-\/]\d{1,2}[-\/]\d{4})\b/)||[])[1]||'';
      const ctx=lines.slice(Math.max(0,i-50),i+3).join('\n');
      const buyDate=latestDate(ctx);
      const navDate=dateInLine||latestDate(l)||'';
      const isin=curISIN||extractISIN(ctx);
      const name=curSchemeName;
      if(!name||name.length<6)continue;
      // Key by ISIN (preferred) or name — Map.set OVERWRITES → last/most-recent wins
      const key=(isin||name.slice(0,50)).toLowerCase().replace(/\s+/g,'');
      fundMap.set(key,{name,isin,folio:curFolio,pan:curPAN,units,avgNav,currentNav:navVal||avgNav,prevNav:navVal||avgNav,navDate,costVal,marketVal,buyDate});
      // DO NOT reset inScheme — same scheme may have more Closing Balance rows
    }
  }

  // Collect all Map entries (last = most recent per scheme)
  for(const b of fundMap.values()){
    seen.add((b.isin||b.name.slice(0,50)).toLowerCase().replace(/\s+/g,''));
    funds.push({name:b.name,amfiCode:'',isin:b.isin,units:b.units,avgNav:b.avgNav,currentNav:b.currentNav,prevNav:b.prevNav,navDate:b.navDate||'',category:'',folio:b.folio,pan:b.pan||'',marketVal:b.marketVal,costVal:b.costVal,sip:0,buyDate:b.buyDate,note:'CAS import',addedAt:new Date().toISOString()});
  }

  /* ── STRATEGY B: Portfolio Summary table scan (MF Central) ──
     Looks for lines that have: scheme name + numbers for units/nav/value ── */
  if(!funds.length){
    const summaryStart=lines.findIndex(l=>/portfolio\s+summary|scheme[-\s]*wise|summary\s+of\s+investments?/i.test(l));
    const scanFrom=summaryStart>=0?summaryStart:0;
    for(let i=scanFrom;i<lines.length;i++){
      const l=lines[i];
      if(/transaction\s+details?|account\s+details?|page\s+\d/i.test(l))break;
      if(isJunk(l))continue;
      const nums=(l.match(/[\d,]+\.?\d*/g)||[]).map(x=>parseFloat(x.replace(/,/g,''))).filter(n=>isFinite(n)&&n>0);
      if(nums.length<2)continue;
      const units=nums[nums.length-1];
      if(!units||units>1e7||units<0.001)continue;
      const marketVal=nums.length>=2?nums[nums.length-2]:0;
      const costVal=nums.length>=3?nums[nums.length-3]:0;
      const navVal=marketVal>0&&units>0?+(marketVal/units).toFixed(4):0;
      const nameM=l.match(/^([A-Za-z\u0900-\u097F][\w\s\-&'',()\.\/:]+?)(?=\s{2,}[\d,]|\s+\d{2,}[\.,])/);
      let name=nameM?nameM[1].replace(/\s{2,}/g,' ').trim():'';
      if(name.length<8){
        for(let j=i-1;j>=Math.max(0,i-8);j--){
          const p=lines[j];
          if(p.length>8&&!isJunk(p)&&!/^[\d]/.test(p)){name=p.replace(/\s{2,}/g,' ').trim();break;}
        }
      }
      if(!name||name.length<6)continue;
      const ctx=lines.slice(Math.max(0,i-6),i+4).join('\n');
      const folio=(ctx.match(/folio\s*(?:no\.?|#)?\s*[:\-]?\s*([A-Z0-9\/\-]{4,})/i)||[])[1]||'';
      const isin=extractISIN(ctx);
      const buyDate=latestDate(ctx);
      const key=(isin||name.slice(0,50)).toLowerCase().replace(/\s+/g,'');
      if(seen.has(key))continue; seen.add(key);
      funds.push({name,amfiCode:'',isin,units,avgNav:costVal>0&&units>0?+(costVal/units).toFixed(4):0,currentNav:navVal,prevNav:navVal,navDate:'',category:'',folio,marketVal,costVal,sip:0,buyDate,note:'CAS import',addedAt:new Date().toISOString()});
    }
  }

  /* ── STRATEGY C: CSV / XLSX with header row ── */
  if(!funds.length){
    const sep=text.includes('\t')?'\t':',';
    const hIdx=lines.findIndex(l=>/fund|scheme|nav|unit|folio|isin/i.test(l)&&l.includes(sep));
    if(hIdx>=0){
      const hdrs=lines[hIdx].split(sep).map(h=>h.replace(/['"]/g,'').trim().toLowerCase());
      const ci=pats=>{for(const p of pats){const idx=hdrs.findIndex(h=>p.test(h));if(idx>=0)return idx;}return -1;};
      const cN=ci([/scheme.*name|fund.*name|name/i]);
      const cU=ci([/closing\s+unit|unit|balance|qty/i]);
      const cI=ci([/isin/i]);
      const cF=ci([/folio/i]);
      const cC=ci([/cost|purchase|invest(?:ed)?/i]);
      const cM=ci([/market|current.*val|value/i]);
      const cNav=ci([/^nav$/i,/nav/i]);
      const cD=ci([/date|purchase\s+date|last\s+(?:purchase|transaction)/i]);
      for(let i=hIdx+1;i<lines.length;i++){
        const p=lines[i].split(sep).map(x=>x.replace(/['"]/g,'').trim());
        if(!p.length||p.every(x=>!x))continue;
        const name=cN>=0?p[cN]||'':''; if(name.length<5)continue;
        const units=cU>=0?num(p[cU]):0; if(!units)continue;
        const isin=cI>=0?(p[cI]||'').toUpperCase().trim():'';
        const folio=cF>=0?p[cF]||'':'';
        const costVal=cC>=0?num(p[cC]):0;
        const marketVal=cM>=0?num(p[cM]):0;
        const navVal=cNav>=0?num(p[cNav]):0;
        const buyDate=cD>=0?p[cD]||'':'';
        const key=((/^IN[A-Z0-9]{10}$/.test(isin)?isin:'')||name.slice(0,50)).toLowerCase().replace(/\s+/g,'');
        if(seen.has(key))continue; seen.add(key);
        funds.push({name,amfiCode:'',isin:/^IN[A-Z0-9]{10}$/.test(isin)?isin:'',units,avgNav:costVal>0&&units>0?+(costVal/units).toFixed(4):0,currentNav:navVal||(marketVal>0&&units>0?+(marketVal/units).toFixed(4):0),prevNav:navVal||(marketVal>0&&units>0?+(marketVal/units).toFixed(4):0),navDate:'',category:'',folio,marketVal,costVal,sip:0,buyDate,note:'CAS import',addedAt:new Date().toISOString()});
      }
    }
  }

  /* ── AMFI VALIDATION PASS — ISIN + AMFI Code both MANDATORY ──
     1. ISIN-first search (most precise match)
     2. Name-based fallback
     3. fetchNAV for latest NAV + date
     Ensures amfiCode is always set (mandatory) and isin is populated.
  ── */
  for(const f of funds.slice(0,80)){
    try{
      let matched=null;
      // Try ISIN first — most precise
      if(/^IN[A-Z0-9]{10}$/.test(f.isin)){
        for(let attempt=0;attempt<2;attempt++){
          try{
            const r=await fetch(`https://api.mfapi.in/mf/search?q=${encodeURIComponent(f.isin)}`,{signal:AbortSignal.timeout(9000)});
            if(!r.ok)throw new Error('http');
            const rs=await r.json();
            if(Array.isArray(rs)&&rs.length){
              matched=rs.find(x=>x.isinGrowth===f.isin||x.isinDividend===f.isin)
                ||rs.find(x=>{const n=(x.schemeName||'').toUpperCase();return n.includes('DIRECT')&&(n.includes('GROWTH')||n.includes(' GR '));})
                ||rs[0];
              if(matched)break;
            }
          }catch{if(attempt===0)await wait(600);}
        }
      }
      // Fallback: name-based search (first 7 words, prefer Direct Growth)
      if(!matched){
        const q=f.name.trim().split(/\s+/).slice(0,7).join(' ');
        for(let attempt=0;attempt<2;attempt++){
          try{
            const r=await fetch(`https://api.mfapi.in/mf/search?q=${encodeURIComponent(q)}`,{signal:AbortSignal.timeout(9000)});
            if(!r.ok)throw new Error('http');
            const rs=await r.json();
            if(Array.isArray(rs)&&rs.length){
              matched=rs.find(x=>{const n=(x.schemeName||'').toUpperCase();return n.includes('DIRECT')&&(n.includes('GROWTH')||n.includes(' GR '));})
                ||rs[0];
              if(matched)break;
            }
          }catch{if(attempt===0)await wait(600);}
        }
      }
      if(matched){
        f.amfiCode=String(matched.schemeCode);
        f.name=matched.schemeName||f.name; // AMFI canonical name
        // Populate ISIN from AMFI if missing
        if(!f.isin&&matched.isinGrowth)f.isin=matched.isinGrowth;
        else if(!f.isin&&matched.isinDividend)f.isin=matched.isinDividend;
        // Fetch live NAV from AMFI
        const nd=await fetchNAV(f.amfiCode);
        if(nd){f.currentNav=nd.nav;f.prevNav=nd.prev;f.navDate=nd.date;if(nd.cat)f.category=nd.cat;}
      }
    }catch{}
    await wait(150);
  }

  return funds.slice(0,500);
}
</script>


<script>
// DEMAT UPLOAD
function handleDematUpload(e){const f=e.target.files?.[0];if(f)parseDematFile(f);e.target.value='';}
function retryDemat(){if(!pendingDemat)return;const pwd=(g('demat-pwd').value||'').trim();if(!pwd){toast('Enter PDF password','err');return;}parseDematFile(pendingDemat,pwd);}
async function parseDematFile(file,password){
  pendingDemat=file;const out=g('demat-pout');
  out.style.display='block';out.className='pout inf';out.textContent='Parsing demat statement…';
  g('demat-pwd-row').classList.remove('show');
  try{
    let text='';
    if(file.name.match(/\.xlsx?$/i)){text=await xlsxToCSV(file);}
    else if(file.name.toLowerCase().endsWith('.pdf')){
      out.textContent='Extracting PDF text…';
      try{text=await extractPDFText(file,password);}
      catch(err){if(err.isPwd){out.className='pout err';out.innerHTML='🔒 Password-protected. Enter password below.';g('demat-pwd-row').classList.add('show');return;}throw err;}
    }else{text=await file.text();}
    const stocks=parseDematText(text);
    if(!stocks.length){out.className='pout err';out.innerHTML='⚠ No stock data found.<br>Download NSDL/CDSL holding statement as CSV and upload here.<br><strong>Columns needed:</strong> ISIN, Company Name, Quantity';return;}
    const m=cm();let added=0,skipped=0;
    for(const s of stocks){const dup=m.stocks.find(x=>x.ticker===s.ticker||(s.isin&&x.isin===s.isin));if(!dup){m.stocks.push(s);added++;}else skipped++;}
    persist();renderAll();
    out.className='pout ok';
    out.innerHTML=`✓ Found ${stocks.length} holding${stocks.length!==1?'s':''}. Added ${added} new${skipped?`, ${skipped} already tracked`:''}.`+`<br><strong>Note: Avg Cost = ${RU}0</strong> — click ✎ on each stock to enter actual purchase price.`;
    if(added>0)setTimeout(()=>refreshStocksOnly(),900);
  }catch(err){out.className='pout err';out.textContent='Error: '+(err.message||String(err));}
}

function parseDematText(raw){
  const stocks=[],seen=new Set();const lines=raw.split(/\r?\n/);
  let headerIdx=-1,headers=[];
  for(let i=0;i<Math.min(40,lines.length);i++){
    const p=lines[i].split(/[,\t]/);
    if(p.some(x=>/isin|company|scrip|security|symbol|quantity|balance|shares/i.test(x.trim()))){headerIdx=i;headers=p.map(x=>x.trim().toLowerCase());break;}
  }
  const colIdx=patterns=>{for(const pat of patterns){const i=headers.findIndex(h=>pat.test(h));if(i>=0)return i;}return-1;};
  if(headerIdx>=0){
    const ciISIN=colIdx([/^isin$/,/isin/]);
    const ciName=colIdx([/company.?name/,/security.?name/,/scrip.?name/,/description/,/company/,/security/,/scrip/,/instrument/]);
    const ciSym=colIdx([/^symbol$/,/trading.?symbol/,/nse.?symbol/,/^ticker$/,/scrip.?code/]);
    const ciQty=colIdx([/net.?qty/,/balance.?qty/,/closing.?qty/,/^qty$/,/quantity/,/^shares$/,/^balance$/,/^holding/,/^units$/]);
    for(let i=headerIdx+1;i<lines.length;i++){
      const p=lines[i].split(/[,\t]/);if(!p.length||p.every(x=>!x.trim()))continue;
      const isin=ciISIN>=0?(p[ciISIN]||'').trim().replace(/['"]/g,''):'';
      const name=ciName>=0?(p[ciName]||'').trim().replace(/['"]/g,''):'';
      const sym=ciSym>=0?(p[ciSym]||'').trim().replace(/['"]/g,''):'';
      const qtyRaw=ciQty>=0?(p[ciQty]||'').trim().replace(/[,'"]/g,''):'';
      const qty=parseFloat(qtyRaw);if(!isFinite(qty)||qty<=0)continue;
      const isinClean=/^IN[A-Z0-9]{10}$/.test(isin)?isin:'';if(!name&&!sym&&!isinClean)continue;
      const match=NSE.find(s=>s.isin===isinClean||(name.length>3&&s.n.toUpperCase().startsWith(name.toUpperCase().slice(0,8)))||(sym.length>2&&s.t===sym.toUpperCase()));
      const ticker=match?match.t:(sym||name).replace(/\s/g,'').replace(/[^A-Z0-9\-&]/gi,'').toUpperCase().slice(0,12);
      const key=(isinClean||ticker).toLowerCase();if(seen.has(key)||!ticker)continue;seen.add(key);
      stocks.push({ticker,name:match?match.n:(name||sym||isinClean),exchange:'NS',isin:isinClean||match?.isin||'',qty,avgPrice:0,currentPrice:0,prevPrice:0,liveOk:false,lastFetch:'',priceSource:null,buyDate:'',note:'NSDL/CDSL import',addedAt:new Date().toISOString()});
    }
  }
  // Fallback ISIN scan
  if(stocks.length===0){
    for(const line of lines){
      if(!line.trim())continue;
      const isinM=line.match(/\b(IN[A-Z0-9]{10})\b/);const isin=isinM?isinM[1]:'';
      const p=line.split(/[,\t]/);
      const nums=p.map(c=>parseFloat(c.replace(/[,₹\s]/g,''))).filter(n=>isFinite(n)&&n>0&&n<1e8);
      const qty=nums.find(n=>Number.isInteger(n))||0;if(!qty&&!isin)continue;
      let name='';
      for(const cell of p){const t=cell.trim().replace(/['"]/g,'');if(t.length<2||/^\d/.test(t)||/^IN[A-Z0-9]/.test(t))continue;if(/^(isin|company|name|qty|balance|market|value|price|date|folio|closing|scrip|symbol|description|total|dr|cr|demat|nsdl|cdsl|holding|equity|units|shares|sl|no|sr)$/i.test(t))continue;if(!name)name=t;}
      if(!name||!qty)continue;
      const match=NSE.find(s=>s.isin===isin||s.n.toUpperCase().startsWith(name.toUpperCase().slice(0,8))||s.t===name.toUpperCase().slice(0,12));
      const ticker=match?match.t:(name).replace(/\s/g,'').replace(/[^A-Z0-9\-&]/gi,'').toUpperCase().slice(0,12);
      const key=(isin||ticker).toLowerCase();if(seen.has(key)||!ticker)continue;seen.add(key);
      stocks.push({ticker,name:match?match.n:name,exchange:'NS',isin:isin||match?.isin||'',qty,avgPrice:0,currentPrice:0,prevPrice:0,liveOk:false,lastFetch:'',priceSource:null,buyDate:'',note:'NSDL/CDSL import',addedAt:new Date().toISOString()});
    }
  }
  return stocks.slice(0,500);
}
</script>


<script>
// BROKER IMPORT — universal, all brokers, all formats, broker-tagged duplicates allowed
function handleBrokerUpload(e){const f=e.target.files?.[0];if(f)parseBrokerFile(f);e.target.value='';}
function retryBroker(){if(!pendingBroker)return;const pwd=(g('broker-pwd').value||'').trim();parseBrokerFile(pendingBroker,pwd);}
async function parseBrokerFile(file,password){
  pendingBroker=file;const out=g('broker-pout');
  out.style.display='block';out.className='pout inf';out.textContent='Parsing broker statement…';
  g('broker-pwd-row').classList.remove('show');
  try{
    let text='';
    if(file.name.match(/\.xlsx?$/i)){
      out.textContent='Reading Excel…';
      const ab=await file.arrayBuffer();
      const wb=XLSX.read(ab,{type:'array'});
      // Try all sheets — some brokers put data on sheet 2+
      text=wb.SheetNames.map(sn=>XLSX.utils.sheet_to_csv(wb.Sheets[sn],{blankrows:false})).join('\n');
    }else if(file.name.toLowerCase().endsWith('.pdf')){
      out.textContent='Extracting PDF…';
      try{text=await extractPDFText(file,password);}
      catch(err){if(err.isPwd){out.className='pout err';out.innerHTML='🔒 Password-protected. Enter password below.';g('broker-pwd-row').classList.add('show');return;}throw err;}
    }else{text=await file.text();}
