  for(const s of m.stocks||[]){const q=sf(s.qty),a=sf(s.avgPrice),c=sf(s.currentPrice,a),vi=q*a,vc=q*c,gn=vc-vi,rt=vi>0?gn/vi*100:0;csv+=`"${s.name}",${s.ticker},${s.isin||''},${q},${a},${c},${vi.toFixed(2)},${vc.toFixed(2)},${gn.toFixed(2)},${rt.toFixed(2)}%,${s.priceSource||'—'}\n`;}
  csv+=`\nBonds\nBond Name,ISIN,Type,No. of Bonds,Face Value,Purchase Price,Coupon%,Rating,Invest Date,Maturity Date\n`;
  for(const b of m.bonds||[]){const inv=sf(b.qty)*sf(b.purchasePrice);csv+=`"${b.name}",${b.isin||''},${BOND_LBL[b.type]||b.type},${b.qty},${b.faceValue},${b.purchasePrice},${b.couponRate||''},${b.rating||''},${b.investDate||''},${b.maturityDate||''}\n`;}
  csv+=`\nInsurance\nHolder,Policy No,Provider,Type,Sum Insured,Premium,Start,End,Due,Nominee\n`;
  for(const p of m.insurance||[]){csv+=`"${p.holder}","${p.policyNum}","${p.provider}",${INS_LBL[p.type]||p.type},${p.sum},${p.premium},${p.startDate},${p.endDate},${p.dueDate},"${p.nominee}"\n`;}
  dlFile('pk-wealthpulse.csv',csv,'text/csv');toast('✓ CSV downloaded','ok');
}

function exportJSON(){
  const m=cm();
  dlFile('pk-wealthpulse-backup.json',JSON.stringify({exportedAt:new Date().toISOString(),member:m.name,pan:maskPAN(m.pan),holdings:m.holdings,stocks:m.stocks,bonds:m.bonds,insurance:m.insurance,bankAccounts:m.bankAccounts,theme:S.theme},null,2),'application/json');
  toast('✓ JSON backup downloaded','ok');
}

function exportXLS(){
  const m=cm();
  let html=`<html><head><meta charset="UTF-8"><style>th{background:#4f52d6;color:#fff;padding:6px 8px;font-size:11px;}td{padding:5px 8px;border:1px solid #ddd;font-size:12px;}</style></head><body>`;
  html+=`<h2>PK WealthPulse — Portfolio Report</h2><p>Generated: ${new Date().toLocaleString('en-IN')} | Member: ${m.name}</p>`;
  html+=`<h3>Mutual Funds</h3><table><tr><th>Fund Name</th><th>AMFI</th><th>Units</th><th>Cost Value</th><th>Market Value</th><th>Gain</th><th>Return%</th></tr>`;
  for(const f of m.holdings||[]){const u=sf(f.units),a=sf(f.avgNav),c=sf(f.currentNav,a),vi=u*a,vc=u*c,gn=vc-vi,rt=vi>0?gn/vi*100:0;html+=`<tr><td>${f.name}</td><td>${f.amfiCode||''}</td><td>${fm(u,4)}</td><td>${fm(vi,2)}</td><td>${fm(vc,2)}</td><td style="color:${gn>=0?'green':'red'}">${gn>=0?'+':''}${fm(gn,2)}</td><td style="color:${rt>=0?'green':'red'}">${rt>=0?'+':''}${fm(rt,2)}%</td></tr>`;}
  html+=`</table><br><h3>Stocks</h3><table><tr><th>Company</th><th>Symbol</th><th>ISIN</th><th>Qty</th><th>Invested</th><th>Mkt Val</th><th>Gain</th><th>Return%</th></tr>`;
  for(const s of m.stocks||[]){const q=sf(s.qty),a=sf(s.avgPrice),c=sf(s.currentPrice,a),vi=q*a,vc=q*c,gn=vc-vi,rt=vi>0?gn/vi*100:0;html+=`<tr><td>${s.name}</td><td>${s.ticker}</td><td>${s.isin||''}</td><td>${q}</td><td>${fm(vi,2)}</td><td>${fm(vc,2)}</td><td style="color:${gn>=0?'green':'red'}">${gn>=0?'+':''}${fm(gn,2)}</td><td style="color:${rt>=0?'green':'red'}">${rt>=0?'+':''}${fm(rt,2)}%</td></tr>`;}
  html+=`</table><br><h3>Bonds</h3><table><tr><th>Bond Name</th><th>ISIN</th><th>Type</th><th>Qty</th><th>Face Val</th><th>Invested</th><th>Coupon%</th><th>Rating</th><th>Maturity</th></tr>`;
  for(const b of m.bonds||[]){const inv=sf(b.qty)*sf(b.purchasePrice);html+=`<tr><td>${b.name}</td><td>${b.isin||''}</td><td>${BOND_LBL[b.type]||b.type}</td><td>${b.qty}</td><td>${fm(b.faceValue,0)}</td><td>${fm(inv,2)}</td><td>${b.couponRate?fm(b.couponRate,2)+'%':'—'}</td><td>${b.rating||'—'}</td><td>${b.maturityDate||'—'}</td></tr>`;}
  html+=`</table><br><h3>Insurance</h3><table><tr><th>Holder</th><th>Policy No</th><th>Provider</th><th>Type</th><th>Sum Insured</th><th>Premium</th><th>Due</th><th>Nominee</th></tr>`;
  for(const p of m.insurance||[]){html+=`<tr><td>${p.holder}</td><td>${p.policyNum}</td><td>${p.provider}</td><td>${INS_LBL[p.type]||p.type}</td><td>${fm(p.sum)}</td><td>${fm(p.premium)}</td><td>${p.dueDate}</td><td>${p.nominee}</td></tr>`;}
  html+=`</table></body></html>`;
  dlFile('pk-wealthpulse-report.xls',html,'application/vnd.ms-excel');toast('✓ Excel downloaded','ok');
}

function exportPDF(){
  const m=cm();
  let mfI=0,mfC=0;for(const f of m.holdings||[]){const u=sf(f.units),a=sf(f.avgNav),c=sf(f.currentNav,a);mfI+=u*a;mfC+=u*c;}
  let skI=0,skC=0;for(const s of m.stocks||[]){const q=sf(s.qty),a=sf(s.avgPrice),c=sf(s.currentPrice,a);skI+=q*a;skC+=q*c;}
  let bndI=0;for(const b of m.bonds||[]){bndI+=sf(b.qty)*sf(b.purchasePrice);}
  const tI=mfI+skI+bndI,tC=mfC+skC+bndI,gain=tC-tI,ret=tI>0?gain/tI*100:0;
  const mfRows=(m.holdings||[]).map(f=>{const u=sf(f.units),a=sf(f.avgNav),c=sf(f.currentNav,a),vi=u*a,vc=u*c,gn=vc-vi,rt=vi>0?gn/vi*100:0;return`<tr><td>${escH(f.name.slice(0,50))}</td><td>${fm(u,4)}</td><td>${fm(vi,2)}</td><td>${fm(vc,2)}</td><td style="color:${gn>=0?'#059669':'#dc2c4a'}">${gn>=0?'+':'-'}${fm(Math.abs(gn),2)}</td><td style="color:${rt>=0?'#059669':'#dc2c4a'}">${rt>=0?'+':''}${fm(rt,2)}%</td></tr>`;}).join('');
  const skRows=(m.stocks||[]).map(s=>{const q=sf(s.qty),a=sf(s.avgPrice),c=sf(s.currentPrice,a),vi=q*a,vc=q*c,gn=vc-vi,rt=vi>0?gn/vi*100:0;return`<tr><td>${escH(s.name)}</td><td>${s.ticker}</td><td>${q}</td><td>${fm(vi,2)}</td><td>${fm(vc,2)}</td><td style="color:${gn>=0?'#059669':'#dc2c4a'}">${gn>=0?'+':'-'}${fm(Math.abs(gn),2)}</td><td style="color:${rt>=0?'#059669':'#dc2c4a'}">${rt>=0?'+':''}${fm(rt,2)}%</td></tr>`;}).join('');
  const bndRows=(m.bonds||[]).map(b=>{const inv=sf(b.qty)*sf(b.purchasePrice);return`<tr><td>${escH(b.name.slice(0,45))}</td><td>${BOND_LBL[b.type]||b.type}</td><td>${b.qty}</td><td>${fm(inv,2)}</td><td>${b.couponRate?fm(b.couponRate,2)+'%':'—'}</td><td>${b.rating||'—'}</td><td>${b.maturityDate||'—'}</td></tr>`;}).join('');
  const insRows=(m.insurance||[]).map(p=>`<tr><td>${escH(p.holder)}</td><td>${escH(p.provider)}</td><td>${INS_LBL[p.type]||p.type}</td><td>${fm(p.sum)}</td><td>${fm(p.premium)}</td><td>${p.dueDate||'—'}</td></tr>`).join('');
  const w=window.open('','_blank','width=960,height=730');
  if(!w){toast('Allow pop-ups to export PDF','err');return;}
  w.document.write(`<!DOCTYPE html><html><head><meta charset="UTF-8"><title>PK WealthPulse Report</title><style>*{box-sizing:border-box;margin:0;padding:0;font-family:Arial,sans-serif;}body{padding:28px;color:#1a1714;font-size:12px;}h1{font-size:20px;color:#4f52d6;margin-bottom:3px;}sub{font-size:11px;color:#a0907a;margin-bottom:18px;display:block;}.summary{display:grid;grid-template-columns:repeat(4,1fr);gap:10px;margin:16px 0 20px;}.sc{background:#f4f1ec;border-radius:7px;padding:11px 13px;}.sc-l{font-size:8px;font-weight:700;text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:.07em;color:#a0907a;margin-bottom:3px;}.sc-v{font-size:18px;font-weight:800;color:#4f52d6;}h2{font-size:13px;font-weight:700;margin:17px 0 7px;color:#1a1714;border-bottom:2px solid #4f52d6;padding-bottom:3px;}table{width:100%;border-collapse:collapse;margin-bottom:18px;}th{background:#4f52d6;color:#fff;padding:6px 8px;font-size:9px;font-weight:700;text-align:left;}td{padding:6px 8px;border-bottom:1px solid #e8e3d8;font-size:11px;}.ft{margin-top:24px;font-size:9px;color:#a0907a;border-top:1px solid #e8e3d8;padding-top:8px;}@media print{@page{margin:12mm;}body{padding:0;}}</style></head><body><h1>PK WealthPulse — Portfolio Report</h1><sub>Member: ${m.name} | Generated: ${new Date().toLocaleString('en-IN')} | Private &amp; Local</sub><div class="summary"><div class="sc"><div class="sc-l">Total Value</div><div class="sc-v">${fL(tC)}</div></div><div class="sc"><div class="sc-l">Invested</div><div class="sc-v" style="color:#0f9b6e">${fL(tI)}</div></div><div class="sc"><div class="sc-l">Gain/Loss</div><div class="sc-v" style="color:${gain>=0?'#0f9b6e':'#dc2c4a'}">${gain>=0?'+':''}${fL(gain)}</div></div><div class="sc"><div class="sc-l">Return</div><div class="sc-v" style="color:${ret>=0?'#0f9b6e':'#dc2c4a'}">${ret>=0?'+':''}${fm(ret,2)}%</div></div></div>${m.holdings?.length?`<h2>Mutual Funds (${m.holdings.length})</h2><table><tr><th>Fund Name</th><th>Units</th><th>Invested</th><th>Current</th><th>Gain</th><th>Return</th></tr>${mfRows}</table>`:''}${m.stocks?.length?`<h2>Stocks (${m.stocks.length})</h2><table><tr><th>Stock</th><th>Ticker</th><th>Qty</th><th>Invested</th><th>Current</th><th>Gain</th><th>Return</th></tr>${skRows}</table>`:''}${m.bonds?.length?`<h2>Bonds (${m.bonds.length})</h2><table><tr><th>Bond Name</th><th>Type</th><th>Qty</th><th>Invested</th><th>Coupon%</th><th>Rating</th><th>Maturity</th></tr>${bndRows}</table>`:''}${m.insurance?.length?`<h2>Insurance (${m.insurance.length})</h2><table><tr><th>Holder</th><th>Provider</th><th>Type</th><th>Sum Insured</th><th>Premium/yr</th><th>Next Due</th></tr>${insRows}</table>`:''}  <div class="ft">PK WealthPulse · Private local tracker · All data on your device</div><script>setTimeout(()=>window.print(),500);<\/script></body></html>`);
  w.document.close();toast('✓ PDF opened — use Ctrl+P / Cmd+P to save as PDF','ok');
}

function importJSON(e){
  const file=e.target.files?.[0];if(!file)return;
  const reader=new FileReader();
  reader.onload=ev=>{
    try{
      const data=JSON.parse(ev.target.result);
      if(!data.holdings&&!data.stocks&&!data.insurance&&!data.bonds){toast('Invalid backup file','err');return;}
      const m=cm();let added=0;
      for(const f of data.holdings||[]){if(!m.holdings.find(h=>h.name===f.name)){m.holdings.push(f);added++;}}
      for(const s of data.stocks||[]){if(!m.stocks.find(x=>x.ticker===s.ticker)){m.stocks.push(s);added++;}}
      for(const b of data.bonds||[]){if(!m.bonds.find(x=>x.isin===b.isin&&x.name===b.name)){m.bonds.push(b);added++;}}
      for(const p of data.insurance||[]){m.insurance.push(p);added++;}
      if(data.theme)setTheme(data.theme);
      persist();renderAll();toast(`✓ Restored ${added} records`,'ok');
    }catch{toast('Could not parse backup file','err');}
  };
  reader.readAsText(file);e.target.value='';
}

function sendEmail(){
  const m=cm();const to=(g('exp-email').value||'').trim();const sub=encodeURIComponent(g('exp-subj').value||'PK WealthPulse Report');
  let mfI=0,mfC=0;for(const f of m.holdings||[]){const u=sf(f.units),a=sf(f.avgNav),c=sf(f.currentNav,a);mfI+=u*a;mfC+=u*c;}
  let skI=0,skC=0;for(const s of m.stocks||[]){const q=sf(s.qty),a=sf(s.avgPrice),c=sf(s.currentPrice,a);skI+=q*a;skC+=q*c;}
  let bndI=0;for(const b of m.bonds||[]){bndI+=sf(b.qty)*sf(b.purchasePrice);}
  const tI=mfI+skI+bndI,tC=mfC+skC+bndI,gain=tC-tI,ret=tI>0?gain/tI*100:0;
  const body=encodeURIComponent(`PK WealthPulse Report\n${'='.repeat(40)}\nGenerated: ${new Date().toLocaleString('en-IN')}\nMember: ${m.name}\n\nTOTAL VALUE: ${fL(tC)}\nInvested: ${fL(tI)}\nReturn: ${(ret>=0?'+':'')+fm(ret,2)}%\nGain: ${gain>=0?'+':''}${fL(gain)}\n\nMF (${m.holdings?.length||0}): ${fL(mfC)} · Stocks (${m.stocks?.length||0}): ${fL(skC)} · Bonds (${m.bonds?.length||0}): ${fL(bndI)}\nInsurance Policies: ${m.insurance?.length||0}\n\nPK WealthPulse — Private & Local`);
  window.location.href=`mailto:${to}?subject=${sub}&body=${body}`;
}

function dlFile(name,content,type){const a=document.createElement('a');a.href=URL.createObjectURL(new Blob([content],{type}));a.download=name;a.click();URL.revokeObjectURL(a.href);}
</script>


<script>
// PAGE NAV / UI
const PAGE_LIST=['portfolio','banks','insurance','family','import','export','profile'];

function showPage(name){
  PAGE_LIST.forEach((p,i)=>{
    const pg=g('page-'+p);if(pg)pg.classList.toggle('active',p===name);
    const tabs=document.querySelectorAll('.tab-btn');if(tabs[i])tabs[i].classList.toggle('active',p===name);
  });
  if(name==='family')renderFamily();
  if(name==='profile')renderProfile();
  if(name==='insurance')renderInsurance();
  if(name==='banks')renderBanks();
}

function showIT(tab){
  ['cas','demat','broker','bonds','portals'].forEach(t=>{
    const panel=g('ip-'+t);if(panel)panel.classList.toggle('active',t===tab);
    const btn=g('it-'+t);if(btn)btn.classList.toggle('active',t===tab);
  });
}

function selP(key){
  document.querySelectorAll('.pb2').forEach(e=>e.classList.remove('sel'));
  const pb=g('pb-'+key);if(pb)pb.classList.add('sel');
  const p=PORTALS[key];if(!p)return;
  const desc=g('pdesc');
  if(desc)desc.innerHTML=`<strong>${p.lbl}</strong><br>${p.txt}<br><br><a href="${p.url}" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><button class="btn btn-p btn-sm">${p.btn}</button></a>`;
}

// OVERLAY / MODAL
function openOv(id){const el=g(id);if(el)el.classList.add('open');}
function closeOv(id){const el=g(id);if(el)el.classList.remove('open');}
document.querySelectorAll('.ov').forEach(el=>el.addEventListener('click',e=>{if(e.target===el)el.classList.remove('open');}));
document.addEventListener('keydown',e=>{if(e.key==='Escape')document.querySelectorAll('.ov.open').forEach(el=>el.classList.remove('open'));});
document.addEventListener('click',e=>{
  if(!e.target.closest('#mf-q')&&!e.target.closest('#mf-sd')){const sd=g('mf-sd');if(sd)sd.classList.remove('open');}
  if(!e.target.closest('#stk-q')&&!e.target.closest('#stk-sd')){const sd=g('stk-sd');if(sd)sd.classList.remove('open');}
});

// TOAST
let _toastT;
function toast(msg,type='ok'){
  const t=g('toast');if(!t)return;t.textContent=msg;t.className=`toast ${type} show`;
  clearTimeout(_toastT);_toastT=setTimeout(()=>t.classList.remove('show'),4000);
}

// UTILS
function getCat(cat,name){
  const c=(cat||'').toLowerCase(),n=(name||'').toLowerCase();
  if(c.includes('flexi cap'))return'Flexi Cap';if(c.includes('large & mid')||c.includes('large and mid'))return'Lg & Mid';
  if(c.includes('large cap'))return'Large Cap';if(c.includes('mid cap'))return'Mid Cap';
  if(c.includes('small cap'))return'Small Cap';if(c.includes('elss')||c.includes('tax sav'))return'ELSS';
  if(c.includes('gold')||n.includes('gold'))return'Gold';if(c.includes('silver')||n.includes('silver'))return'Silver';
  if(c.includes('international')||c.includes('global')||n.includes('nasdaq')||n.includes('us equity'))return'Intl';
  if(c.includes('index')||n.includes('index')||n.includes('nifty')||n.includes('sensex'))return'Index';
  if(c.includes('sectoral')||c.includes('thematic'))return'Sectoral';
  if(c.includes('focused'))return'Focused';if(c.includes('multi cap'))return'Multi Cap';
  if(c.includes('value')||c.includes('contra'))return'Value';
  if(c.includes('debt')||c.includes('liquid')||c.includes('bond')||c.includes('overnight')||c.includes('money market'))return'Debt';
  if(c.includes('hybrid')||c.includes('balanced'))return'Hybrid';
  return'Equity';
}

// AUTO-BOOT
(function autoboot(){
  if(S.pan&&S.members&&S.members[S.pan]){
    g('login-screen').style.display='none';g('app-screen').style.display='block';
    const m=S.members[S.pan];g('tb-name').textContent=m.name.split(' ')[0];g('tb-pan').textContent=maskPAN(S.pan);panVis=false;
    setTheme((S.theme&&S.theme!=='system')?S.theme:'light');
    selP('mfc');renderAll();
    if((m.holdings||[]).length||(m.stocks||[]).length)refreshAll(true);
  }
})();
